1254 
1303 __kernel void gemm_mm_reshaped_only_rhs_t(IMAGE_DECLARATION(lhs),
1304  IMAGE_DECLARATION(rhs),
1305  IMAGE_DECLARATION(dst),
1306  uint lhs_stride_z,
1307  uint rhs_stride_z,
1308  uint dst_stride_z
1309 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
1310  ,
1311  uint lhs_cross_plane_pad
1312 #endif // REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D
1313 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
1314  ,
1315  uint dst_cross_plane_pad
1316 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
1317  )
1318 {
1319  // Block size
1320 #define RHS_BLOCK_SIZE ((K0) * (N0))
1321 
1322  // RHS offset and step X
1323 #if defined(RHS_INTERLEAVE)
1324 #define RHS_OFFSET_X (K0)
1325 #define RHS_STEP_X ((K0) * (H0))
1326 #define RHS_STEP_LOOP (1)
1327 #else // defined(RHS_INTERLEAVE)
1328 #define RHS_OFFSET_X (RHS_BLOCK_SIZE)
1329 #define RHS_STEP_X (K0)
1330 #define RHS_STEP_LOOP (H0)
1331 #endif // defined(RHS_INTERLEAVE)
1332 
1333  uint x = get_global_id(0);
1334  uint y = get_global_id(1);
1335  uint z = get_global_id(2);
1336 
1337 #if defined(DUMMY_WORK_ITEMS)
1338  if((x * N0 >= N) || (y * M0 >= M))
1339  {
1340  return;
1341  }
1342 #endif // defined(DUMMY_WORK_ITEMS)
1343 
1344  // Compute LHS matrix address
1345  uint lhs_offset = lhs_offset_first_element_in_bytes + y * M0 * (uint)lhs_stride_y;
1346 
1347  // Compute RHS matrix address
1348  uint rhs_offset = rhs_offset_first_element_in_bytes + (x % H0) * (uint)RHS_OFFSET_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE) + (x / (uint)H0) * rhs_stride_y;
1349 
1350 #if defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
1351  // Do not slide matrix B if the matrix B has 3 dimensions and matrix A more than 3
1352  rhs_offset += (z % MATRIX_B_DEPTH) * rhs_stride_z;
1353 #else // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
1354  rhs_offset += z * rhs_stride_z;
1355 #endif // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
1356 
1357  REPEAT_VAR_INIT_TO_CONST(8, uint, zin, 0); //uint zout0=0,zout1=0,zout2=0,... zout7=0;
1358 
1359 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
1360  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
1361  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
1362  //
1363  // | |
1364  // | plane0 |
1365  // | |
1366  // |__________________|
1367  // |******************|
1368  // | cross_plane_pad |
1369  // |******************|
1370  // | |
1371  // | plane1 |
1372  // | |
1373  // |__________________|
1374 
1375  // The plane (zin) is calculated dividing M (y * M0) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
1376  zin0 = (0 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1377  zin0 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin0);
1378  zin0 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1379 #if M0 > 1
1380  zin1 = (1 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1381  zin1 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin1);
1382  zin1 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1383 #endif // M0 > 1
1384 #if M0 > 2
1385  zin2 = (2 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1386  zin2 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin2);
1387  zin2 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1388 #endif // M0 > 2
1389 #if M0 > 3
1390  zin3 = (3 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1391  zin3 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin3);
1392  zin3 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1393 #endif // M0 > 3
1394 #if M0 > 4
1395  zin4 = (4 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1396  zin4 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin4);
1397  zin4 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1398 #endif // M0 > 4
1399 #if M0 > 5
1400  zin5 = (5 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1401  zin5 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin5);
1402  zin5 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1403 #endif // M0 > 5
1404 #if M0 > 6
1405  zin6 = (6 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1406  zin6 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin6);
1407  zin6 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1408 #endif // M0 > 6
1409 #if M0 > 7
1410  zin7 = (7 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1411  zin7 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout7);
1412  zin7 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1413 #endif // M0 > 7
1414 
1415  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
1416  // multiply lhs_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
1417  lhs_offset += z * lhs_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
1418 
1419 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
1420 
1421  // Add offset for batched GEMM
1422  lhs_offset += z * lhs_stride_z;
1423 
1424 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
1425 
1426  // Initialize the accumulators
1427  REPEAT_VAR_INIT_TO_CONST(M0, VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0), c, 0); //VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0) c0=0,c1=0,c2=0,... c(M0-1)=0;
1428 
1429  int i = 0;
1430  for(; i <= (K - K0); i += K0)
1431  {
1432  // Supported cases (M0, K0):
1433  // 1,2 - 1,3 - 1,4 - 1,8 - 1,16
1434  // 2,2 - 2,3 - 2,4 - 2,8 - 2,16
1435  // 3,2 - 3,3 - 3,4 - 3,8 - 3,16
1436  // 4,2 - 4,3 - 4,4 - 4,8 - 4,16
1437  // 5,2 - 5,3 - 5,4 - 5,8 - 5,16
1438  // 6,2 - 6,3 - 6,4 - 6,8 - 6,16
1439  // 7,2 - 7,3 - 7,4 - 7,8 - 7,16
1440  // 8,2 - 8,3 - 8,4 - 8,8 - 8,16
1441  // Load values from LHS matrix
1442  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1443  a0 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 0 * lhs_stride_y + zin0));
1444 #if M0 > 1
1445  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1446  a1 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 1 * lhs_stride_y + zin1));
1447 #endif // M0 > 1
1448 #if M0 > 2
1449  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1450  a2 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 2 * lhs_stride_y + zin2));
1451 #endif // M0 > 2
1452 #if M0 > 3
1453  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1454  a3 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 3 * lhs_stride_y + zin3));
1455 #endif // M0 > 3
1456 #if M0 > 4
1457  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1458  a4 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 4 * lhs_stride_y + zin4));
1459 #endif // M0 > 4
1460 #if M0 > 5
1461  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1462  a5 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 5 * lhs_stride_y + zin5));
1463 #endif // M0 > 5
1464 #if M0 > 6
1465  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1466  a6 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 6 * lhs_stride_y + zin6));
1467 #endif // M0 > 6
1468 #if M0 > 7
1469  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1470  a7 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 7 * lhs_stride_y + zin7));
1471 #endif // M0 > 7
1472 
1473  // Load values from RHS matrix
1474  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1475  b0 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 0 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1476  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1477  b1 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 1 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1478 #if N0 > 2
1479  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1480  b2 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 2 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1481 #endif // N0 > 2
1482 #if N0 > 3
1483  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1484  b3 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 3 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1485 #endif // N0 > 3
1486 #if N0 > 4
1487  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1488  b4 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 4 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1489  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1490  b5 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 5 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1491  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1492  b6 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 6 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1493  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1494  b7 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 7 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1495 #endif // N0 > 4
1496 #if N0 > 8
1497  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1498  b8 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 8 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1499  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1500  b9 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 9 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1501  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1502  bA = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 10 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1503  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1504  bB = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 11 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1505  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1506  bC = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 12 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1507  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1508  bD = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 13 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1509  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1510  bE = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 14 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1511  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
1512  bF = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 15 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1513 #endif // N0 > 8
1514 
1515  // Accumulate
1516  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(K0, a0, b, c0);
1517 #if M0 > 1
1518  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(K0, a1, b, c1);
1519 #endif // M0 > 1
1520 #if M0 > 2
1521  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(K0, a2, b, c2);
1522 #endif // M0 > 2
1523 #if M0 > 3
1524  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(K0, a3, b, c3);
1525 #endif // M0 > 3
1526 #if M0 > 4
1527  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(K0, a4, b, c4);
1528 #endif // M0 > 4
1529 #if M0 > 5
1530  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(K0, a5, b, c5);
1531 #endif // M0 > 5
1532 #if M0 > 6
1533  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(K0, a6, b, c6);
1534 #endif // M0 > 6
1535 #if M0 > 7
1536  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(K0, a7, b, c7);
1537 #endif // M0 > 7
1538 
1539  lhs_offset += K0 * sizeof(DATA_TYPE);
1540  rhs_offset += (N0 * RHS_STEP_X * RHS_STEP_LOOP) * sizeof(DATA_TYPE);
1541  }
1542 
1543  // Left-over accumulations
1544  for(; i < K; ++i)
1545  {
1546  // Load values from LHS matrix
1547  DATA_TYPE a0 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 0 * lhs_stride_y + zin0));
1548 #if M0 > 1
1549  DATA_TYPE a1 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 1 * lhs_stride_y + zin1));
1550 #endif // M0 > 1
1551 #if M0 > 2
1552  DATA_TYPE a2 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 2 * lhs_stride_y + zin2));
1553 #endif // M0 > 2
1554 #if M0 > 3
1555  DATA_TYPE a3 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 3 * lhs_stride_y + zin3));
1556 #endif // M0 > 3
1557 #if M0 > 4
1558  DATA_TYPE a4 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 4 * lhs_stride_y + zin4));
1559 #endif // M0 > 4
1560 #if M0 > 5
1561  DATA_TYPE a5 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 5 * lhs_stride_y + zin5));
1562 #endif // M0 > 5
1563 #if M0 > 6
1564  DATA_TYPE a6 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 6 * lhs_stride_y + zin6));
1565 #endif // M0 > 6
1566 #if M0 > 7
1567  DATA_TYPE a7 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 7 * lhs_stride_y + zin7));
1568 #endif // M0 > 7
1569 
1570  // Load values from RHS matrix
1571  DATA_TYPE b0 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 0 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1572  DATA_TYPE b1 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 1 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1573 #if N0 > 2
1574  DATA_TYPE b2 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 2 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1575 #endif // N0 > 2
1576 #if N0 > 3
1577  DATA_TYPE b3 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 3 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1578 #endif // N0 > 3
1579 #if N0 > 4
1580  DATA_TYPE b4 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 4 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1581  DATA_TYPE b5 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 5 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1582  DATA_TYPE b6 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 6 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1583  DATA_TYPE b7 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 7 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1584 #endif // N0 > 4
1585 #if N0 > 8
1586  DATA_TYPE b8 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 8 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1587  DATA_TYPE b9 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 9 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1588  DATA_TYPE bA = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 10 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1589  DATA_TYPE bB = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 11 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1590  DATA_TYPE bC = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 12 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1591  DATA_TYPE bD = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 13 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1592  DATA_TYPE bE = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 14 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1593  DATA_TYPE bF = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 15 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
1594 #endif // N0 > 8
1595 
1596  // Accumulate
1597  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(1, a0, b, c0);
1598 #if M0 > 1
1599  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(1, a1, b, c1);
1600 #endif // M0 > 1
1601 #if M0 > 2
1602  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(1, a2, b, c2);
1603 #endif // M0 > 2
1604 #if M0 > 3
1605  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(1, a3, b, c3);
1606 #endif // M0 > 3
1607 #if M0 > 4
1608  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(1, a4, b, c4);
1609 #endif // M0 > 4
1610 #if M0 > 5
1611  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(1, a5, b, c5);
1612 #endif // M0 > 5
1613 #if M0 > 6
1614  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(1, a6, b, c6);
1615 #endif // M0 > 6
1616 #if M0 > 7
1617  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(1, a7, b, c7);
1618 #endif // M0 > 7
1619 
1620  lhs_offset += sizeof(DATA_TYPE);
1621  rhs_offset += sizeof(DATA_TYPE);
1622  }
1623 
1624  __global uchar *dst_addr = dst_ptr + dst_offset_first_element_in_bytes + (x * (uint)N0 * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)) + (y * (uint)M0 * dst_stride_y);
1625 
1626  REPEAT_VAR_INIT_TO_CONST(8, uint, zout, 0); //uint zout0=0,zout1=0,zout2=0,... zout7=0;
1627 
1628 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
1629  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
1630  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
1631  //
1632  // | |
1633  // | plane0 |
1634  // | |
1635  // |__________________|
1636  // |******************|
1637  // | cross_plane_pad |
1638  // |******************|
1639  // | |
1640  // | plane1 |
1641  // | |
1642  // |__________________|
1643 
1644  // The plane (zout) is calculated dividing M (y * M0) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
1645  zout0 = (0 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1646  zout0 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout0);
1647  zout0 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
1648 #if M0 > 1
1649  zout1 = (1 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1650  zout1 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout1);
1651  zout1 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
1652 #endif // M0 > 1
1653 #if M0 > 2
1654  zout2 = (2 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1655  zout2 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout2);
1656  zout2 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
1657 #endif // M0 > 2
1658 #if M0 > 3
1659  zout3 = (3 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1660  zout3 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout3);
1661  zout3 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
1662 #endif // M0 > 3
1663 #if M0 > 4
1664  zout4 = (4 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1665  zout4 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout4);
1666  zout4 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
1667 #endif // M0 > 4
1668 #if M0 > 5
1669  zout5 = (5 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1670  zout5 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout5);
1671  zout5 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
1672 #endif // M0 > 5
1673 #if M0 > 6
1674  zout6 = (6 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1675  zout6 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout6);
1676  zout6 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
1677 #endif // M0 > 6
1678 #if M0 > 7
1679  zout7 = (7 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1680  zout7 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout7);
1681  zout7 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
1682 #endif // M0 > 7
1683 
1684  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
1685  // multiply dst_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
1686  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
1687 
1688 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
1689 
1690  // Add offset for batched GEMM
1691  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z;
1692 
1693 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
1694 
1695  // Multiply by the weight of matrix-matrix product and store the result
1696 #if defined(ALPHA)
1697  c0 = c0 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
1698 #if M0 > 1
1699  c1 = c1 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
1700 #endif // M0 > 1
1701 #if M0 > 2
1702  c2 = c2 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
1703 #endif // M0 > 2
1704 #if M0 > 3
1705  c3 = c3 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
1706 #endif // M0 > 3
1707 #if M0 > 4
1708  c4 = c4 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
1709 #endif // M0 > 4
1710 #if M0 > 5
1711  c5 = c5 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
1712 #endif // M0 > 5
1713 #if M0 > 6
1714  c6 = c6 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
1715 #endif // M0 > 5
1716 #if M0 > 7
1717  c7 = c7 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
1718 #endif // M0 > 7
1719 #endif // defined(ALPHA)
1720 
1721  // Store output block
1722  VSTORE(N0)
1723  (c0, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y + zout0));
1724 #if M0 > 1
1725  VSTORE(N0)
1726  (c1, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y + zout1));
1727 #endif // M0 > 1
1728 #if M0 > 2
1729  VSTORE(N0)
1730  (c2, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y + zout2));
1731 #endif // M0 > 2
1732 #if M0 > 3
1733  VSTORE(N0)
1734  (c3, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y + zout3));
1735 #endif // M0 > 3
1736 #if M0 > 4
1737  VSTORE(N0)
1738  (c4, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 4 * dst_stride_y + zout4));
1739 #endif // M0 > 4
1740 #if M0 > 5
1741  VSTORE(N0)
1742  (c5, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 5 * dst_stride_y + zout5));
1743 #endif // M0 > 5
1744 #if M0 > 6
1745  VSTORE(N0)
1746  (c6, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 6 * dst_stride_y + zout6));
1747 #endif // M0 > 6
1748 #if M0 > 7
1749  VSTORE(N0)
1750  (c7, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 7 * dst_stride_y + zout7));
1751 #endif // M0 > 7
1752 
1753 #undef RHS_BLOCK_SIZE
1754 #undef RHS_OFFSET_X
1755 #undef RHS_STEP_X
1756 }
1757 
1758 #define VFMA(a, b, c) \
1759  ({ \
1760  c = fma(a, b, c); \
1761  })
1762 
1763 #if M0 == 1
1764 #define LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(i, a, c) \
1765  ({ \
1766  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0) \
1767  b = VLOAD(N0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 0x##i * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE))); \
1768  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##0).s##i), b, (c##0)); \
1769  })
1770 #elif M0 == 2 // M0 == 2
1771 #define LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(i, a, c) \
1772  ({ \
1773  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0) \
1774  b = VLOAD(N0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 0x##i * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE))); \
1775  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##0).s##i), b, (c##0)); \
1776  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##1).s##i), b, (c##1)); \
1777  })
1778 #elif M0 == 3 // M0 == 3
1779 #define LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(i, a, c) \
1780  ({ \
1781  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0) \
1782  b = VLOAD(N0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 0x##i * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE))); \
1783  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##0).s##i), b, (c##0)); \
1784  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##1).s##i), b, (c##1)); \
1785  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##2).s##i), b, (c##2)); \
1786  })
1787 #elif M0 == 4 // M0 == 4
1788 #define LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(i, a, c) \
1789  ({ \
1790  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0) \
1791  b = VLOAD(N0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 0x##i * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE))); \
1792  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##0).s##i), b, (c##0)); \
1793  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##1).s##i), b, (c##1)); \
1794  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##2).s##i), b, (c##2)); \
1795  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##3).s##i), b, (c##3)); \
1796  })
1797 #elif M0 == 5 // M0 == 5
1798 #define LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(i, a, c) \
1799  ({ \
1800  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0) \
1801  b = VLOAD(N0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 0x##i * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE))); \
1802  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##0).s##i), b, (c##0)); \
1803  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##1).s##i), b, (c##1)); \
1804  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##2).s##i), b, (c##2)); \
1805  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##3).s##i), b, (c##3)); \
1806  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##4).s##i), b, (c##4)); \
1807  })
1808 #elif M0 == 6 // M0 == 6
1809 #define LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(i, a, c) \
1810  ({ \
1811  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0) \
1812  b = VLOAD(N0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 0x##i * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE))); \
1813  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##0).s##i), b, (c##0)); \
1814  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##1).s##i), b, (c##1)); \
1815  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##2).s##i), b, (c##2)); \
1816  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##3).s##i), b, (c##3)); \
1817  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##4).s##i), b, (c##4)); \
1818  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##5).s##i), b, (c##5)); \
1819  })
1820 #elif M0 == 7 // M0 == 7
1821 #define LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(i, a, c) \
1822  ({ \
1823  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0) \
1824  b = VLOAD(N0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 0x##i * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE))); \
1825  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##0).s##i), b, (c##0)); \
1826  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##1).s##i), b, (c##1)); \
1827  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##2).s##i), b, (c##2)); \
1828  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##3).s##i), b, (c##3)); \
1829  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##4).s##i), b, (c##4)); \
1830  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##5).s##i), b, (c##5)); \
1831  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##6).s##i), b, (c##6)); \
1832  })
1833 #elif M0 == 8 // M0 == 8
1834 #define LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(i, a, c) \
1835  ({ \
1836  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0) \
1837  b = VLOAD(N0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_ptr + rhs_offset + 0x##i * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE))); \
1838  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##0).s##i), b, (c##0)); \
1839  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##1).s##i), b, (c##1)); \
1840  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##2).s##i), b, (c##2)); \
1841  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##3).s##i), b, (c##3)); \
1842  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##4).s##i), b, (c##4)); \
1843  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##5).s##i), b, (c##5)); \
1844  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##6).s##i), b, (c##6)); \
1845  VFMA((VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0))((a##7).s##i), b, (c##7)); \
1846  })
1847 #else // M0 not supported
1848 #error "M0 not supported"
1849 #endif // M0 not supported
1850 
1898 __kernel void gemm_mm_reshaped_only_rhs_nt(IMAGE_DECLARATION(lhs),
1899  IMAGE_DECLARATION(rhs),
1900  IMAGE_DECLARATION(dst),
1901  uint lhs_stride_z,
1902  uint rhs_stride_z,
1903  uint dst_stride_z
1904 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
1905  ,
1906  uint lhs_cross_plane_pad
1907 #endif // REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D
1908 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
1909  ,
1910  uint dst_cross_plane_pad
1911 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
1912  )
1913 {
1914  // Block size
1915 #define RHS_BLOCK_SIZE ((K0) * (N0))
1916 
1917  // RHS offset and step X
1918 #if defined(RHS_INTERLEAVE)
1919 #define RHS_OFFSET_X (N0)
1920 #define RHS_STEP_X ((N0) * (H0))
1921 #define RHS_STEP_LOOP (1)
1922 #else // defined(RHS_INTERLEAVE)
1923 #define RHS_OFFSET_X (RHS_BLOCK_SIZE)
1924 #define RHS_STEP_X (N0)
1925 #define RHS_STEP_LOOP (H0)
1926 #endif // defined(RHS_INTERLEAVE)
1927 
1928  uint x = get_global_id(0);
1929  uint y = get_global_id(1);
1930  uint z = get_global_id(2);
1931 
1932 #if defined(DUMMY_WORK_ITEMS)
1933  if((x * N0 >= N) || (y * M0 >= M))
1934  {
1935  return;
1936  }
1937 #endif // defined(DUMMY_WORK_ITEMS)
1938 
1939  // Compute LHS matrix address
1940  uint lhs_offset = lhs_offset_first_element_in_bytes + y * M0 * (uint)lhs_stride_y;
1941 
1942  // Compute RHS matrix address
1943  uint rhs_offset = rhs_offset_first_element_in_bytes + (x % H0) * (uint)RHS_OFFSET_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE) + (x / (uint)H0) * rhs_stride_y;
1944 
1945 #if defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
1946  // Do not slide matrix B if the matrix B has 3 dimensions and matrix A more than 3
1947  rhs_offset += (z % MATRIX_B_DEPTH) * rhs_stride_z;
1948 #else // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
1949  rhs_offset += z * rhs_stride_z;
1950 #endif // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
1951 
1952  REPEAT_VAR_INIT_TO_CONST(8, uint, zin, 0); //uint zout0=0,zout1=0,zout2=0,... zout7=0;
1953 
1954 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
1955  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
1956  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
1957  //
1958  // | |
1959  // | plane0 |
1960  // | |
1961  // |__________________|
1962  // |******************|
1963  // | cross_plane_pad |
1964  // |******************|
1965  // | |
1966  // | plane1 |
1967  // | |
1968  // |__________________|
1969 
1970  // The plane (zin) is calculated dividing M (y * M0) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
1971  zin0 = (0 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1972  zin0 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin0);
1973  zin0 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1974 #if M0 > 1
1975  zin1 = (1 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1976  zin1 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin1);
1977  zin1 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1978 #endif // M0 > 1
1979 #if M0 > 2
1980  zin2 = (2 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1981  zin2 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin2);
1982  zin2 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1983 #endif // M0 > 2
1984 #if M0 > 3
1985  zin3 = (3 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1986  zin3 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin3);
1987  zin3 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1988 #endif // M0 > 3
1989 #if M0 > 4
1990  zin4 = (4 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1991  zin4 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin4);
1992  zin4 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1993 #endif // M0 > 4
1994 #if M0 > 5
1995  zin5 = (5 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
1996  zin5 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin5);
1997  zin5 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
1998 #endif // M0 > 5
1999 #if M0 > 6
2000  zin6 = (6 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2001  zin6 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zin6);
2002  zin6 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
2003 #endif // M0 > 6
2004 #if M0 > 7
2005  zin7 = (7 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2006  zin7 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout7);
2007  zin7 *= (lhs_cross_plane_pad * lhs_stride_y);
2008 #endif // M0 > 7
2009 
2010  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
2011  // multiply lhs_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
2012  lhs_offset += z * lhs_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
2013 
2014 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
2015 
2016  // Add offset for batched GEMM
2017  lhs_offset += z * lhs_stride_z;
2018 
2019 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
2020 
2021  // Initialize the accumulators
2022  REPEAT_VAR_INIT_TO_CONST(M0, VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0), c, 0); //VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0) c0=0,c1=0,c2=0,... c(N0-1)=0;
2023 
2024  int i = 0;
2025  for(; i <= (K - K0); i += K0)
2026  {
2027  // Supported cases (M0, K0):
2028  // 1,2 - 1,3 - 1,4 - 1,8 - 1,16
2029  // 2,2 - 2,3 - 2,4 - 2,8 - 2,16
2030  // 3,2 - 3,3 - 3,4 - 3,8 - 3,16
2031  // 4,2 - 4,3 - 4,4 - 4,8 - 4,16
2032  // 5,2 - 5,3 - 5,4 - 5,8 - 5,16
2033  // 6,2 - 6,3 - 6,4 - 6,8 - 6,16
2034  // 7,2 - 7,3 - 7,4 - 7,8 - 7,16
2035  // 8,2 - 8,3 - 8,4 - 8,8 - 8,16
2036  // Load values from LHS matrix
2037  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2038  a0 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 0 * lhs_stride_y + zin0));
2039 #if M0 > 1
2040  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2041  a1 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 1 * lhs_stride_y + zin1));
2042 #endif // M0 > 1
2043 #if M0 > 2
2044  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2045  a2 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 2 * lhs_stride_y + zin2));
2046 #endif // M0 > 2
2047 #if M0 > 3
2048  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2049  a3 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 3 * lhs_stride_y + zin3));
2050 #endif // M0 > 3
2051 #if M0 > 4
2052  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2053  a4 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 4 * lhs_stride_y + zin4));
2054 #endif // M0 > 4
2055 #if M0 > 5
2056  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2057  a5 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 5 * lhs_stride_y + zin5));
2058 #endif // M0 > 5
2059 #if M0 > 6
2060  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2061  a6 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 6 * lhs_stride_y + zin6));
2062 #endif // M0 > 6
2063 #if M0 > 7
2064  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2065  a7 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 7 * lhs_stride_y + zin7));
2066 #endif // M0 > 7
2067 
2068  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(0, a, c);
2069  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(1, a, c);
2070 #if K0 > 2
2071  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(2, a, c);
2072 #endif // K0 > 2
2073 #if K0 > 3
2074  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(3, a, c);
2075 #endif // K0 > 3
2076 #if K0 > 4
2077  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(4, a, c);
2078  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(5, a, c);
2079  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(6, a, c);
2080  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(7, a, c);
2081 #endif // K0 > 4
2082 #if K0 > 8
2083  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(8, a, c);
2084  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(9, a, c);
2085  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(A, a, c);
2086  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(B, a, c);
2087  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(C, a, c);
2088  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(D, a, c);
2089  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(E, a, c);
2090  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(F, a, c);
2091 #endif // K0 > 8
2092 
2093  lhs_offset += K0 * sizeof(DATA_TYPE);
2094  rhs_offset += K0 * RHS_STEP_X * RHS_STEP_LOOP * sizeof(DATA_TYPE);
2095  }
2096 
2097  // Left-over accumulations
2098  for(; i < K; ++i)
2099  {
2100  // Load values from LHS matrix
2101  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
2102  a0 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 0 * lhs_stride_y + zin0));
2103 #if M0 > 1
2104  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
2105  a1 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 1 * lhs_stride_y + zin1));
2106 #endif // M0 > 1
2107 #if M0 > 2
2108  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
2109  a2 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 2 * lhs_stride_y + zin2));
2110 #endif // M0 > 2
2111 #if M0 > 3
2112  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
2113  a3 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 3 * lhs_stride_y + zin3));
2114 #endif // M0 > 3
2115 #if M0 > 4
2116  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
2117  a4 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 4 * lhs_stride_y + zin4));
2118 #endif // M0 > 4
2119 #if M0 > 5
2120  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
2121  a5 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 5 * lhs_stride_y + zin5));
2122 #endif // M0 > 5
2123 #if M0 > 6
2124  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
2125  a6 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 6 * lhs_stride_y + zin6));
2126 #endif // M0 > 6
2127 #if M0 > 7
2128  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
2129  a7 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_ptr + lhs_offset + 7 * lhs_stride_y + zin));
2130 #endif // M0 > 7
2131 
2132  LD_RHS_VFMA_M0xN0(0, a, c);
2133 
2134  lhs_offset += sizeof(DATA_TYPE);
2135  rhs_offset += RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE);
2136  }
2137 
2138  __global uchar *dst_addr = dst_ptr + dst_offset_first_element_in_bytes + (x * (uint)N0 * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)) + (y * (uint)M0 * dst_stride_y);
2139 
2140  REPEAT_VAR_INIT_TO_CONST(8, uint, zout, 0); //uint zout0=0,zout1=0,zout2=0,... zout7=0;
2141 
2142 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
2143  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
2144  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
2145  //
2146  // | |
2147  // | plane0 |
2148  // | |
2149  // |__________________|
2150  // |******************|
2151  // | cross_plane_pad |
2152  // |******************|
2153  // | |
2154  // | plane1 |
2155  // | |
2156  // |__________________|
2157 
2158  // The plane (zout) is calculated dividing M (y * M0) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
2159  zout0 = (0 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2160  zout0 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout0);
2161  zout0 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2162 #if M0 > 1
2163  zout1 = (1 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2164  zout1 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout1);
2165  zout1 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2166 #endif // M0 > 1
2167 #if M0 > 2
2168  zout2 = (2 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2169  zout2 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout2);
2170  zout2 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2171 #endif // M0 > 2
2172 #if M0 > 3
2173  zout3 = (3 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2174  zout3 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout3);
2175  zout3 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2176 #endif // M0 > 3
2177 #if M0 > 4
2178  zout4 = (4 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2179  zout4 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout4);
2180  zout4 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2181 #endif // M0 > 4
2182 #if M0 > 5
2183  zout5 = (5 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2184  zout5 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout5);
2185  zout5 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2186 #endif // M0 > 5
2187 #if M0 > 6
2188  zout6 = (6 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2189  zout6 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout6);
2190  zout6 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2191 #endif // M0 > 6
2192 #if M0 > 7
2193  zout7 = (7 + (uint)(y * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2194  zout7 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout7);
2195  zout7 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2196 #endif // M0 > 7
2197 
2198  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
2199  // multiply dst_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
2200  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
2201 
2202 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
2203 
2204  // Add offset for batched GEMM
2205  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z;
2206 
2207 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
2208 
2209  // Multiply by the weight of matrix-matrix product and store the result
2210 #if defined(ALPHA)
2211  c0 = c0 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2212 #if M0 > 1
2213  c1 = c1 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2214 #endif // M0 > 1
2215 #if M0 > 2
2216  c2 = c2 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2217 #endif // M0 > 2
2218 #if M0 > 3
2219  c3 = c3 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2220 #endif // M0 > 3
2221 #if M0 > 4
2222  c4 = c4 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2223 #endif // M0 > 4
2224 #if M0 > 5
2225  c5 = c5 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2226 #endif // M0 > 5
2227 #if M0 > 6
2228  c6 = c6 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2229 #endif // M0 > 5
2230 #if M0 > 7
2231  c7 = c7 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2232 #endif // M0 > 7
2233 #endif // defined(ALPHA)
2234 
2235  // Store output block
2236  VSTORE(N0)
2237  (c0, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y + zout0));
2238 #if M0 > 1
2239  VSTORE(N0)
2240  (c1, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y + zout1));
2241 #endif // M0 > 1
2242 #if M0 > 2
2243  VSTORE(N0)
2244  (c2, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y + zout2));
2245 #endif // M0 > 2
2246 #if M0 > 3
2247  VSTORE(N0)
2248  (c3, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y + zout3));
2249 #endif // M0 > 3
2250 #if M0 > 4
2251  VSTORE(N0)
2252  (c4, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 4 * dst_stride_y + zout4));
2253 #endif // M0 > 4
2254 #if M0 > 5
2255  VSTORE(N0)
2256  (c5, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 5 * dst_stride_y + zout5));
2257 #endif // M0 > 5
2258 #if M0 > 6
2259  VSTORE(N0)
2260  (c6, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 6 * dst_stride_y + zout6));
2261 #endif // M0 > 6
2262 #if M0 > 7
2263  VSTORE(N0)
2264  (c7, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 7 * dst_stride_y + zout7));
2265 #endif // M0 > 7
2266 
2267 #undef RHS_BLOCK_SIZE
2268 #undef RHS_OFFSET_X
2269 #undef RHS_STEP_X
2270 }
2271 #endif // defined(M0) && defined(N0) && defined(K0) && defined(H0) && defined(DATA_TYPE) && defined(M) && defined(N) && defined(K)
2272 
2273 #if defined(M0) && defined(N0) && defined(K0) && defined(V0) && defined(H0) && defined(DATA_TYPE) && defined(M) && defined(N)
2274 
2275 #if K0 == 2
2276 #define ARM_DOT_K0(a, b, c) \
2277  ({ \
2278  c = fma(a.s0, b.s0, c); \
2279  c = fma(a.s1, b.s1, c); \
2280  })
2281 #elif K0 == 3 // K0 == 3
2282 #define ARM_DOT_K0(a, b, c) \
2283  ({ \
2284  c = fma(a.s0, b.s0, c); \
2285  c = fma(a.s1, b.s1, c); \
2286  c = fma(a.s2, b.s2, c); \
2287  })
2288 #elif K0 == 4 // K0 == 4
2289 #define ARM_DOT_K0(a, b, c) \
2290  ({ \
2291  c = fma(a.s0, b.s0, c); \
2292  c = fma(a.s1, b.s1, c); \
2293  c = fma(a.s2, b.s2, c); \
2294  c = fma(a.s3, b.s3, c); \
2295  })
2296 #elif K0 == 8 // K0 == 8
2297 #define ARM_DOT_K0(a, b, c) \
2298  ({ \
2299  c = fma(a.s0, b.s0, c); \
2300  c = fma(a.s1, b.s1, c); \
2301  c = fma(a.s2, b.s2, c); \
2302  c = fma(a.s3, b.s3, c); \
2303  c = fma(a.s4, b.s4, c); \
2304  c = fma(a.s5, b.s5, c); \
2305  c = fma(a.s6, b.s6, c); \
2306  c = fma(a.s7, b.s7, c); \
2307  })
2308 #elif K0 == 16 // K0 == 16
2309 #define ARM_DOT_K0(a, b, c) \
2310  ({ \
2311  c = fma(a.s0, b.s0, c); \
2312  c = fma(a.s1, b.s1, c); \
2313  c = fma(a.s2, b.s2, c); \
2314  c = fma(a.s3, b.s3, c); \
2315  c = fma(a.s4, b.s4, c); \
2316  c = fma(a.s5, b.s5, c); \
2317  c = fma(a.s6, b.s6, c); \
2318  c = fma(a.s7, b.s7, c); \
2319  c = fma(a.s8, b.s8, c); \
2320  c = fma(a.s9, b.s9, c); \
2321  c = fma(a.sA, b.sA, c); \
2322  c = fma(a.sB, b.sB, c); \
2323  c = fma(a.sC, b.sC, c); \
2324  c = fma(a.sD, b.sD, c); \
2325  c = fma(a.sE, b.sE, c); \
2326  c = fma(a.sF, b.sF, c); \
2327  })
2328 #else // K0 not supported
2329 #error "K0 value not supported"
2330 #endif // K0 conditions
2331 
2332 #if N0 == 2
2333 #define ARM_DOT_K0XN0(a, b, c) \
2334  ({ \
2335  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##0), (c.s0)); \
2336  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##1), (c.s1)); \
2337  })
2338 #elif N0 == 3 // N0 == 3
2339 #define ARM_DOT_K0XN0(a, b, c) \
2340  ({ \
2341  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##0), (c.s0)); \
2342  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##1), (c.s1)); \
2343  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##2), (c.s2)); \
2344  })
2345 #elif N0 == 4 // N0 == 4
2346 #define ARM_DOT_K0XN0(a, b, c) \
2347  ({ \
2348  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##0), (c.s0)); \
2349  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##1), (c.s1)); \
2350  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##2), (c.s2)); \
2351  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##3), (c.s3)); \
2352  })
2353 #elif N0 == 8 // N0 == 8
2354 #define ARM_DOT_K0XN0(a, b, c) \
2355  ({ \
2356  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##0), (c.s0)); \
2357  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##1), (c.s1)); \
2358  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##2), (c.s2)); \
2359  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##3), (c.s3)); \
2360  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##4), (c.s4)); \
2361  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##5), (c.s5)); \
2362  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##6), (c.s6)); \
2363  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##7), (c.s7)); \
2364  })
2365 #elif N0 == 16 // N0 == 16
2366 #define ARM_DOT_K0XN0(a, b, c) \
2367  ({ \
2368  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##0), (c.s0)); \
2369  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##1), (c.s1)); \
2370  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##2), (c.s2)); \
2371  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##3), (c.s3)); \
2372  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##4), (c.s4)); \
2373  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##5), (c.s5)); \
2374  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##6), (c.s6)); \
2375  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##7), (c.s7)); \
2376  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##8), (c.s8)); \
2377  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##9), (c.s9)); \
2378  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##A), (c.sA)); \
2379  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##B), (c.sB)); \
2380  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##C), (c.sC)); \
2381  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##D), (c.sD)); \
2382  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##E), (c.sE)); \
2383  ARM_DOT_K0((a), (b##F), (c.sF)); \
2384  })
2385 #else // N0 not supported
2386 #error "N0 value not supported"
2387 #endif // N0 conditions
2388 
2437 __kernel void gemm_mm_reshaped_lhs_nt_rhs_t(IMAGE_DECLARATION(lhs),
2438  IMAGE_DECLARATION(rhs),
2439  IMAGE_DECLARATION(dst),
2440  uint k,
2441  uint lhs_stride_z,
2442  uint rhs_stride_z,
2443  uint dst_stride_z
2444 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
2445  ,
2446  uint dst_cross_plane_pad
2447 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
2448  )
2449 {
2450  // Block size
2451 #define LHS_BLOCK_SIZE ((K0) * (M0))
2452 
2453 #if defined(LHS_INTERLEAVE)
2454 #define LHS_OFFSET_X (K0)
2455 #define LHS_STEP_X ((K0) * (V0))
2456 #define LHS_STEP_LOOP (1)
2457 #else // defined(INTERLEAVE)
2458 #define LHS_OFFSET_X (LHS_BLOCK_SIZE)
2459 #define LHS_STEP_X (K0)
2460 #define LHS_STEP_LOOP (V0)
2461 #endif // defined(INTERLEAVE)
2462 
2463  // Block size
2464 #define RHS_BLOCK_SIZE ((K0) * (N0))
2465 
2466  // RHS offset and step X
2467 #if defined(RHS_INTERLEAVE)
2468 #define RHS_OFFSET_X (K0)
2469 #define RHS_STEP_X ((K0) * (H0))
2470 #define RHS_STEP_LOOP (1)
2471 #else // defined(RHS_INTERLEAVE)
2472 #define RHS_OFFSET_X (RHS_BLOCK_SIZE)
2473 #define RHS_STEP_X (K0)
2474 #define RHS_STEP_LOOP (H0)
2475 #endif // defined(RHS_INTERLEAVE)
2476 
2477 #if defined(DUMMY_WORK_ITEMS)
2478  if((get_global_id(0) * N0 >= N) || (get_global_id(1) * M0 >= M))
2479  {
2480  return;
2481  }
2482 #endif // defined(DUMMY_WORK_ITEMS)
2483 
2484  // Compute LHS matrix address
2485  __global uchar *lhs_addr = lhs_ptr + lhs_offset_first_element_in_bytes + (get_global_id(1) % V0) * (uint)LHS_OFFSET_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE) + (get_global_id(1) / V0) * (uint)lhs_stride_y +
2486  (get_global_id(2) * lhs_stride_z);
2487 
2488  // Compute RHS matrix address
2489  __global uchar *rhs_addr = rhs_ptr + rhs_offset_first_element_in_bytes + (get_global_id(0) % H0) * (uint)RHS_OFFSET_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE) + (get_global_id(0) / (uint)H0) * rhs_stride_y;
2490 
2491 #if defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
2492  // Do not slide matrix B if the matrix B has 3 dimensions and matrix A more than 3
2493  rhs_addr += (get_global_id(2) % MATRIX_B_DEPTH) * rhs_stride_z;
2494 #else // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
2495  rhs_addr += get_global_id(2) * rhs_stride_z;
2496 #endif // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
2497 
2498  // Initialize the accumulators
2499  REPEAT_VAR_INIT_TO_CONST(M0, VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0), c, 0); //VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, N0) c0=0,c1=0,c2=0,... c(M0-1)=0;
2500 
2501  for(int i = 0; i < k; i += K0)
2502  {
2503  // Supported cases (M0, K0):
2504  // 1,2 - 1,3 - 1,4 - 1,8 - 1,16
2505  // 2,2 - 2,3 - 2,4 - 2,8 - 2,16
2506  // 3,2 - 3,3 - 3,4 - 3,8 - 3,16
2507  // 4,2 - 4,3 - 4,4 - 4,8 - 4,16
2508  // 5,2 - 5,3 - 5,4 - 5,8 - 5,16
2509  // 6,2 - 6,3 - 6,4 - 6,8 - 6,16
2510  // 7,2 - 7,3 - 7,4 - 7,8 - 7,16
2511  // 8,2 - 8,3 - 8,4 - 8,8 - 8,16
2512  // Load values from LHS matrix
2513  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2514  a0 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_addr + 0 * LHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2515 #if M0 > 1
2516  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2517  a1 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_addr + 1 * LHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2518 #endif // M0 > 1
2519 #if M0 > 2
2520  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2521  a2 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_addr + 2 * LHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2522 #endif // M0 > 2
2523 #if M0 > 3
2524  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2525  a3 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_addr + 3 * LHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2526 #endif // M0 > 3
2527 #if M0 > 4
2528  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2529  a4 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_addr + 4 * LHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2530 #endif // M0 > 4
2531 #if M0 > 5
2532  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2533  a5 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_addr + 5 * LHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2534 #endif // M0 > 5
2535 #if M0 > 6
2536  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2537  a6 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_addr + 6 * LHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2538 #endif // M0 > 6
2539 #if M0 > 7
2540  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2541  a7 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(lhs_addr + 7 * LHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2542 #endif // M0 > 7
2543 
2544  // Load values from RHS matrix
2545  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2546  b0 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 0 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2547  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2548  b1 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 1 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2549 #if N0 > 2
2550  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2551  b2 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 2 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2552 #endif // N0 > 2
2553 #if N0 > 3
2554  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2555  b3 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 3 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2556 #endif // N0 > 3
2557 #if N0 > 4
2558  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2559  b4 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 4 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2560  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2561  b5 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 5 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2562  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2563  b6 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 6 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2564  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2565  b7 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 7 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2566 #endif // N0 > 4
2567 #if N0 > 8
2568  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2569  b8 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 8 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2570  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2571  b9 = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 9 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2572  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2573  bA = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 10 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2574  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2575  bB = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 11 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2576  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2577  bC = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 12 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2578  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2579  bD = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 13 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2580  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2581  bE = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 14 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2582  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, K0)
2583  bF = VLOAD(K0)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(rhs_addr + 15 * RHS_STEP_X * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)));
2584 #endif // N0 > 8
2585 
2586  // Accumulate
2587  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(a0, b, c0);
2588 #if M0 > 1
2589  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(a1, b, c1);
2590 #endif // M0 > 1
2591 #if M0 > 2
2592  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(a2, b, c2);
2593 #endif // M0 > 2
2594 #if M0 > 3
2595  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(a3, b, c3);
2596 #endif // M0 > 3
2597 #if M0 > 4
2598  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(a4, b, c4);
2599 #endif // M0 > 4
2600 #if M0 > 5
2601  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(a5, b, c5);
2602 #endif // M0 > 5
2603 #if M0 > 6
2604  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(a6, b, c6);
2605 #endif // M0 > 6
2606 #if M0 > 7
2607  ARM_DOT_K0XN0(a7, b, c7);
2608 #endif // M0 > 7
2609 
2610  lhs_addr += (M0 * LHS_STEP_X * LHS_STEP_LOOP) * sizeof(DATA_TYPE);
2611  rhs_addr += (N0 * RHS_STEP_X * RHS_STEP_LOOP) * sizeof(DATA_TYPE);
2612  }
2613 
2614  __global uchar *dst_addr = dst_ptr + dst_offset_first_element_in_bytes + (get_global_id(0) * (uint)N0 * sizeof(DATA_TYPE)) + (get_global_id(1) * (uint)M0 * dst_stride_y);
2615 
2616  REPEAT_VAR_INIT_TO_CONST(8, uint, zout, 0); //uint zout0=0,zout1=0,zout2=0,... zout7=0;
2617 
2618 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
2619  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
2620  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
2621  //
2622  // | |
2623  // | plane0 |
2624  // | |
2625  // |__________________|
2626  // |******************|
2627  // | cross_plane_pad |
2628  // |******************|
2629  // | |
2630  // | plane1 |
2631  // | |
2632  // |__________________|
2633 
2634  // The plane (zin) is calculated dividing M (y * M0) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
2635  zout0 = (0 + (uint)(get_global_id(1) * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2636  zout0 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout0);
2637  zout0 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2638 #if M0 > 1
2639  zout1 = (1 + (uint)(get_global_id(1) * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2640  zout1 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout1);
2641  zout1 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2642 #endif // M0 > 1
2643 #if M0 > 2
2644  zout2 = (2 + (uint)(get_global_id(1) * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2645  zout2 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout2);
2646  zout2 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2647 #endif // M0 > 2
2648 #if M0 > 3
2649  zout3 = (3 + (uint)(get_global_id(1) * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2650  zout3 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout3);
2651  zout3 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2652 #endif // M0 > 3
2653 #if M0 > 4
2654  zout4 = (4 + (uint)(get_global_id(1) * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2655  zout4 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout4);
2656  zout4 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2657 #endif // M0 > 4
2658 #if M0 > 5
2659  zout5 = (5 + (uint)(get_global_id(1) * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2660  zout5 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout5);
2661  zout5 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2662 #endif // M0 > 5
2663 #if M0 > 6
2664  zout6 = (6 + (uint)(get_global_id(1) * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2665  zout6 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout6);
2666  zout6 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2667 #endif // M0 > 6
2668 #if M0 > 7
2669  zout7 = (7 + (uint)(get_global_id(1) * (uint)M0)) / (uint)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2670  zout7 = min((uint)(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1), zout7);
2671  zout7 *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
2672 #endif // M0 > 7
2673 
2674  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
2675  // multiply dst_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
2676  dst_addr += get_global_id(2) * dst_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
2677 
2678 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
2679 
2680  // Add offset for batched GEMM
2681  dst_addr += get_global_id(2) * dst_stride_z;
2682 
2683 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
2684 
2685  // Multiply by the weight of matrix-matrix product and store the result
2686 #if defined(ALPHA)
2687  c0 = c0 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2688 #if M0 > 1
2689  c1 = c1 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2690 #endif // M0 > 1
2691 #if M0 > 2
2692  c2 = c2 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2693 #endif // M0 > 2
2694 #if M0 > 3
2695  c3 = c3 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2696 #endif // M0 > 3
2697 #if M0 > 4
2698  c4 = c4 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2699 #endif // M0 > 4
2700 #if M0 > 5
2701  c5 = c5 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2702 #endif // M0 > 5
2703 #if M0 > 6
2704  c6 = c6 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2705 #endif // M0 > 5
2706 #if M0 > 7
2707  c7 = c7 * (DATA_TYPE)ALPHA;
2708 #endif // M0 > 7
2709 #endif // defined(ALPHA)
2710 
2711  // Store output block
2712  VSTORE(N0)
2713  (c0, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y + zout0));
2714 #if M0 > 1
2715  VSTORE(N0)
2716  (c1, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y + zout1));
2717 #endif // M0 > 1
2718 #if M0 > 2
2719  VSTORE(N0)
2720  (c2, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y + zout2));
2721 #endif // M0 > 2
2722 #if M0 > 3
2723  VSTORE(N0)
2724  (c3, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y + zout3));
2725 #endif // M0 > 3
2726 #if M0 > 4
2727  VSTORE(N0)
2728  (c4, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 4 * dst_stride_y + zout4));
2729 #endif // M0 > 4
2730 #if M0 > 5
2731  VSTORE(N0)
2732  (c5, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 5 * dst_stride_y + zout5));
2733 #endif // M0 > 5
2734 #if M0 > 6
2735  VSTORE(N0)
2736  (c6, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 6 * dst_stride_y + zout6));
2737 #endif // M0 > 6
2738 #if M0 > 7
2739  VSTORE(N0)
2740  (c7, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 7 * dst_stride_y + zout7));
2741 #endif // M0 > 7
2742 
2743 #undef LHS_BLOCK_SIZE
2744 #undef LHS_OFFSET_X
2745 #undef LHS_STEP_X
2746 #undef RHS_BLOCK_SIZE
2747 #undef RHS_OFFSET_X
2748 #undef RHS_STEP_X
2749 }
2750 #endif // defined(M0) && defined(N0) && defined(K0) && defined(V0) && defined(H0) && defined(K) && defined(DATA_TYPE)
2751 
2752 #if defined(TRANSPOSE_W) && defined(MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH)
2753 
2754 #if ELEMENT_SIZE == 1
2755 #define DATA_TYPE uchar
2756 #elif ELEMENT_SIZE == 2
2757 #define DATA_TYPE ushort
2758 #elif ELEMENT_SIZE == 4
2759 #define DATA_TYPE uint
2760 #else // ELEMENT_SIZE == 1
2761 #error "Element size not supported"
2762 #endif // ELEMENT_SIZE
2763 
2786 __kernel void gemm_transpose1xW(TENSOR3D_DECLARATION(src),
2787  TENSOR3D_DECLARATION(dst))
2788 {
2789  uint x = get_global_id(0);
2790  uint y = get_global_id(1);
2791  uint z = get_global_id(2);
2792 
2793  // Compute address for Matrix B - source
2794  Tensor3D src = CONVERT_TO_TENSOR3D_STRUCT(src);
2795 
2796  // Compute address for Matrix B transposed - destination. X and Y are swapped
2797  uint dst_addr_in_bytes = dst_offset_first_element_in_bytes + y * TRANSPOSE_W * sizeof(DATA_TYPE) * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH + (x / MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH) * dst_stride_y +
2798  (x % MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH) * TRANSPOSE_W * sizeof(DATA_TYPE);
2799 
2800  // Add offset for batched GEMM
2801  dst_addr_in_bytes += z * dst_stride_z;
2802 
2803  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, TRANSPOSE_W)
2804  b0 = VLOAD(TRANSPOSE_W)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)src.ptr);
2805 
2806  VSTORE(TRANSPOSE_W)
2807  (b0, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_ptr + dst_addr_in_bytes));
2808 }
2809 #endif // defined(TRANSPOSE_W) && defined(MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH)
2810 
2811 #if defined(MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT) && defined(DATA_TYPE)
2812 
2842 __kernel void gemm_interleave4x4(TENSOR3D_DECLARATION(src),
2843  TENSOR3D_DECLARATION(dst)
2844 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
2845  ,
2846  uint cross_plane_pad
2847 #endif // REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D
2848  )
2849 {
2850  // Compute source and destination addresses
2851  uint x = get_global_id(0);
2852  uint y = get_global_id(1);
2853  uint z = get_global_id(2);
2854 
2855  // Compute address for source tensor
2856  Tensor3D src = CONVERT_TO_TENSOR3D_STRUCT(src);
2857 
2858  // Compute address for Matrix B transposed - destination. X and Y are swapped
2859  uint dst_addr_in_bytes = dst_offset_first_element_in_bytes + x * sizeof(DATA_TYPE) * 16 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT + (y / MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT) * dst_stride_y +
2860  (y % MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT) * 4 * sizeof(DATA_TYPE);
2861 
2862  // Add offset for batched GEMM
2863  dst_addr_in_bytes += z * dst_stride_z;
2864 
2865 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
2866  __global uchar *input_ptr = src_ptr + src_offset_first_element_in_bytes + x * 4 * sizeof(DATA_TYPE) + y * 4 * src_stride_y;
2867 
2868  // Since we load a 2D input tile from a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
2869  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
2870  //
2871  // | |
2872  // | plane0 |
2873  // | |
2874  // |__________________|
2875  // |******************|
2876  // | cross_plane_pad |
2877  // |******************|
2878  // | |
2879  // | plane1 |
2880  // | |
2881  // |__________________|
2882 
2883  // The plane (zin) is calculated dividing M (y * 4) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
2884  uint4 zin = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(y * 4)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
2885  zin = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zin);
2886 
2887  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
2888  zin *= (cross_plane_pad * src_stride_y);
2889 
2890  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
2891  // multiply src_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
2892  input_ptr += z * src_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
2893 
2894  // Load values from Matrix A
2895  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 4)
2896  a0 = vload4(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(input_ptr + 0 * src_stride_y + zin.s0));
2897  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 4)
2898  a1 = vload4(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(input_ptr + 1 * src_stride_y + zin.s1));
2899  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 4)
2900  a2 = vload4(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(input_ptr + 2 * src_stride_y + zin.s2));
2901  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 4)
2902  a3 = vload4(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(input_ptr + 3 * src_stride_y + zin.s3));
2903 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
2904  __global uchar *input_ptr = src.ptr;
2905 
2906  // Load values from Matrix A
2907  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 4)
2908  a0 = vload4(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(input_ptr + 0 * src_stride_y));
2909  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 4)
2910  a1 = vload4(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(input_ptr + 1 * src_stride_y));
2911  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 4)
2912  a2 = vload4(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(input_ptr + 2 * src_stride_y));
2913  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 4)
2914  a3 = vload4(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(input_ptr + 3 * src_stride_y));
2915 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
2916 
2917 #if defined(UNROLL_BLOCK)
2918  vstore4(a0, 0, ((__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_ptr + dst_addr_in_bytes) + 0 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT));
2919  vstore4(a1, 0, ((__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_ptr + dst_addr_in_bytes) + 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT));
2920  vstore4(a2, 0, ((__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_ptr + dst_addr_in_bytes) + 8 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT));
2921  vstore4(a3, 0, ((__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_ptr + dst_addr_in_bytes) + 12 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT));
2922 #else // defined(UNROLL_BLOCK)
2923  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 4)
2924  val0 = (VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 4))(a0.s0, a1.s0, a2.s0, a3.s0);
2925  vstore4(val0, 0, ((__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_ptr + dst_addr_in_bytes) + 0 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT));
2926 
2927  val0 = (VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 4))(a0.s1, a1.s1, a2.s1, a3.s1);
2928  vstore4(val0, 0, ((__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_ptr + dst_addr_in_bytes) + 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT));
2929 
2930  val0 = (VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 4))(a0.s2, a1.s2, a2.s2, a3.s2);
2931  vstore4(val0, 0, ((__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_ptr + dst_addr_in_bytes) + 8 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT));
2932 
2933  val0 = (VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 4))(a0.s3, a1.s3, a2.s3, a3.s3);
2934  vstore4(val0, 0, ((__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_ptr + dst_addr_in_bytes) + 12 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT));
2935 #endif // defined(UNROLL_BLOCK)
2936 }
2937 #endif // defined(MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT) && defined(DATA_TYPE)
2938 
2939 #if defined(COLS_B) && defined(MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH) && defined(MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT)
2940 
2986 __kernel void gemm_mm_interleaved_transposed_f32(IMAGE_DECLARATION(src0),
2987  IMAGE_DECLARATION(src1),
2988 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
2989  VECTOR_DECLARATION(src2),
2990 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
2991  IMAGE_DECLARATION(dst),
2992  uint src0_stride_z,
2993  uint src1_stride_z,
2994  uint dst_stride_z
2995 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
2996  ,
2997  uint cross_plane_pad
2998 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
2999  )
3000 {
3001  int x = get_global_id(0) / MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
3002  int y = get_global_id(1) / MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;
3003  int z = get_global_id(2);
3004 
3005  // Offset
3006  const int offset_row_a = (get_global_id(1) % MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT) * 4;
3007  const int offset_row_b = (get_global_id(0) % MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH) * 4;
3008 
3009  // src_addr_a = address of matrix A
3010  // src_addr_b = address of matrix B
3011  int src0_addr_in_bytes = z * src0_stride_z + y * src0_stride_y + src0_offset_first_element_in_bytes;
3012  int src1_addr_in_bytes = x * src1_stride_y + src1_offset_first_element_in_bytes;
3013 
3014 #if defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
3015  // Do not slide matrix B if the matrix B has 3 dimensions and matrix A more than 3
3016  src1_addr_in_bytes += (z % MATRIX_B_DEPTH) * src1_stride_z;
3017 #else // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
3018  src1_addr_in_bytes += z * src1_stride_z;
3019 #endif // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
3020 
3021  __global float *src_addr_a = (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src0_addr_in_bytes);
3022  __global float *src_addr_b = (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src1_addr_in_bytes);
3023 
3024  // Compute end row address for matrix B
3025  __global float *src_end_addr_b = src_addr_b + COLS_B;
3026 
3027  src_addr_a += offset_row_a;
3028  src_addr_b += offset_row_b;
3029 
3030  // Reset accumulators
3031  float4 c00 = 0.0f;
3032  float4 c10 = 0.0f;
3033  float4 c20 = 0.0f;
3034  float4 c30 = 0.0f;
3035 
3036  for(; src_addr_b <= (src_end_addr_b - (int)(8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH)); src_addr_a += 8 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT, src_addr_b += 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH)
3037  {
3038  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
3039  float4 a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a);
3040  float4 b0 = vload4(0, src_addr_b);
3041 
3042  c00 += (float4)a0.s0 * b0;
3043  c10 += (float4)a0.s1 * b0;
3044  c20 += (float4)a0.s2 * b0;
3045  c30 += (float4)a0.s3 * b0;
3046 
3047  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
3048  a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a + 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT);
3049  b0 = vload4(0, src_addr_b + 4 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH);
3050 
3051  c00 += (float4)a0.s0 * b0;
3052  c10 += (float4)a0.s1 * b0;
3053  c20 += (float4)a0.s2 * b0;
3054  c30 += (float4)a0.s3 * b0;
3055  }
3056 
3057  for(; src_addr_b < src_end_addr_b; src_addr_a += 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT, src_addr_b += 4 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH)
3058  {
3059  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
3060  float4 a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a);
3061  float4 b0 = vload4(0, src_addr_b);
3062 
3063  c00 += (float4)a0.s0 * b0;
3064  c10 += (float4)a0.s1 * b0;
3065  c20 += (float4)a0.s2 * b0;
3066  c30 += (float4)a0.s3 * b0;
3067  }
3068 
3069  // Compute destination address
3070  Image dst = CONVERT_TO_IMAGE_STRUCT(dst);
3071 
3072 #if defined(ALPHA)
3073  // Multiply by the weight of matrix product
3074  c00 = c00 * (float4)ALPHA;
3075  c10 = c10 * (float4)ALPHA;
3076  c20 = c20 * (float4)ALPHA;
3077  c30 = c30 * (float4)ALPHA;
3078 #endif // defined(ALPHA)
3079 
3080 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
3081  __global float *src2_addr = (__global float *)(src2_ptr + src2_offset_first_element_in_bytes + get_global_id(0) * src2_step_x);
3082  float4 c0 = vload4(0, src2_addr);
3083 
3084  c00 += c0;
3085  c10 += c0;
3086  c20 += c0;
3087  c30 += c0;
3088 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
3089 
3090  // Compute dst address
3091  __global uchar *dst_addr = offset(&dst, 0, 0);
3092 
3093 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3094  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
3095  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
3096  //
3097  // | |
3098  // | plane0 |
3099  // | |
3100  // |__________________|
3101  // |******************|
3102  // | cross_plane_pad |
3103  // |******************|
3104  // | |
3105  // | plane1 |
3106  // | |
3107  // |__________________|
3108 
3109  // The plane (zout) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * 4) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
3110  uint4 zout = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * 4)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
3111  zout = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zout);
3112 
3113  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
3114  zout *= (cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
3115 
3116  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
3117  // multiply dst_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
3118  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
3119 
3120  // Store 4x4 block
3121  vstore4(c00, 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y + zout.s0));
3122  vstore4(c10, 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y + zout.s1));
3123  vstore4(c20, 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y + zout.s2));
3124  vstore4(c30, 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y + zout.s3));
3125 
3126 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3127  // Add offset for batched GEMM
3128  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z;
3129 
3130  // Store 4x4 block
3131  vstore4(c00, 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y));
3132  vstore4(c10, 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y));
3133  vstore4(c20, 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y));
3134  vstore4(c30, 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y));
3135 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3136 }

3185 __kernel void gemm_mm_interleaved_transposed_f32_bifrost(IMAGE_DECLARATION(src0),

3187 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
3188  VECTOR_DECLARATION(src2),
3189 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
3190  IMAGE_DECLARATION(dst),

3192  uint src1_stride_z,

3194 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)

3233  float c12 = 0.0f;

3236  float c21 = 0.0f;

3241  float c32 = 0.0f;

3250  float4 a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a);

3302 
3303  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
3304  a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a);
3305  b0 = vload4(0, src_addr_b);
3306 
3307  src_addr_a += 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;
3308  src_addr_b += 4 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
3309 
3310  c00 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s0, c00);
3311  c01 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s1, c01);
3312  c02 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s2, c02);
3313  c03 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s3, c03);
3314 
3315  c10 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s0, c10);
3316  c11 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s1, c11);
3317  c12 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s2, c12);
3318  c13 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s3, c13);
3319 
3320  c20 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s0, c20);
3321  c21 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s1, c21);
3322  c22 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s2, c22);
3323  c23 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s3, c23);
3324 
3325  c30 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s0, c30);
3326  c31 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s1, c31);
3327  c32 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s2, c32);
3328  c33 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s3, c33);
3329 
3330  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
3331  a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a);
3332  b0 = vload4(0, src_addr_b);
3333 
3334  src_addr_a += 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;
3335  src_addr_b += 4 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
3336 
3337  c00 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s0, c00);
3338  c01 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s1, c01);
3339  c02 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s2, c02);
3340  c03 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s3, c03);
3341 
3342  c10 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s0, c10);
3343  c11 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s1, c11);
3344  c12 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s2, c12);
3345  c13 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s3, c13);
3346 
3347  c20 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s0, c20);
3348  c21 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s1, c21);
3349  c22 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s2, c22);
3350  c23 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s3, c23);
3351 
3352  c30 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s0, c30);
3353  c31 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s1, c31);
3354  c32 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s2, c32);
3355  c33 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s3, c33);
3356  }
3357 
3358  for(; i < (int)(COLS_MTX_B); ++i)
3359  {
3360  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
3361  float4 a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a);
3362  float4 b0 = vload4(0, src_addr_b);
3363 
3364  src_addr_a += 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;
3365  src_addr_b += 4 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
3366 
3367  c00 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s0, c00);
3368  c01 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s1, c01);
3369  c02 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s2, c02);
3370  c03 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s3, c03);
3371 
3372  c10 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s0, c10);
3373  c11 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s1, c11);
3374  c12 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s2, c12);
3375  c13 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s3, c13);
3376 
3377  c20 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s0, c20);
3378  c21 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s1, c21);
3379  c22 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s2, c22);
3380  c23 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s3, c23);
3381 
3382  c30 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s0, c30);
3383  c31 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s1, c31);
3384  c32 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s2, c32);
3385  c33 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s3, c33);
3386  }
3387 
3388  // Compute destination address
3389  Image dst = CONVERT_TO_IMAGE_STRUCT(dst);
3390 
3391 #if defined(ALPHA)
3392  // Multiply by the weight of matrix product
3393  c00 = c00 * ALPHA;
3394  c01 = c01 * ALPHA;
3395  c02 = c02 * ALPHA;
3396  c03 = c03 * ALPHA;
3397  c10 = c10 * ALPHA;
3398  c11 = c11 * ALPHA;
3399  c12 = c12 * ALPHA;
3400  c13 = c13 * ALPHA;
3401  c20 = c20 * ALPHA;
3402  c21 = c21 * ALPHA;
3403  c22 = c22 * ALPHA;
3404  c23 = c23 * ALPHA;
3405  c30 = c30 * ALPHA;
3406  c31 = c31 * ALPHA;
3407  c32 = c32 * ALPHA;
3408  c33 = c33 * ALPHA;
3409 #endif // defined(ALPHA)
3410 
3411  // Compute dst address
3412  __global uchar *dst_addr = offset(&dst, 0, 0);
3413 
3414 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
3415  __global float *src2_addr = (__global float *)(src2_ptr + src2_offset_first_element_in_bytes + get_global_id(0) * src2_step_x);
3416  float4 c0 = vload4(0, src2_addr);
3417 
3418  c00 += c0.s0;
3419  c01 += c0.s1;
3420  c02 += c0.s2;
3421  c03 += c0.s3;
3422  c10 += c0.s0;
3423  c11 += c0.s1;
3424  c12 += c0.s2;
3425  c13 += c0.s3;
3426  c20 += c0.s0;
3427  c21 += c0.s1;
3428  c22 += c0.s2;
3429  c23 += c0.s3;
3430  c30 += c0.s0;
3431  c31 += c0.s1;
3432  c32 += c0.s2;
3433  c33 += c0.s3;
3434 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
3435 
3436 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3437  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
3438  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
3439  //
3440  // | |
3441  // | plane0 |
3442  // | |
3443  // |__________________|
3444  // |******************|
3445  // | cross_plane_pad |
3446  // |******************|
3447  // | |
3448  // | plane1 |
3449  // | |
3450  // |__________________|
3451 
3452  // The plane (zout) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * 4) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
3453  uint4 zout = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * 4)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
3454  zout = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zout);
3455 
3456  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
3457  zout *= (cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
3458 
3459  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
3460  // multiply dst_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
3461  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
3462 
3463  // Store 4x4 block
3464  vstore4((float4)(c00, c01, c02, c03), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y + zout.s0));
3465  vstore4((float4)(c10, c11, c12, c13), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y + zout.s1));
3466  vstore4((float4)(c20, c21, c22, c23), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y + zout.s2));
3467  vstore4((float4)(c30, c31, c32, c33), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y + zout.s3));
3468 
3469 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3470  // Add offset for batched GEMM
3471  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z;
3472 
3473  // Store 4x4 block
3474  vstore4((float4)(c00, c01, c02, c03), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y));
3475  vstore4((float4)(c10, c11, c12, c13), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y));
3476  vstore4((float4)(c20, c21, c22, c23), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y));
3477  vstore4((float4)(c30, c31, c32, c33), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y));
3478 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3479 }
3480 
3481 // Undefine local defines
3482 #undef COLS_MTX_B
3483 
3484 #if defined(ARM_COMPUTE_OPENCL_FP16_ENABLED)
3485 
3531 __kernel void gemm_mm_interleaved_transposed_f16(IMAGE_DECLARATION(src0),
3532  IMAGE_DECLARATION(src1),
3533 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
3534  VECTOR_DECLARATION(src2),
3535 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
3536  IMAGE_DECLARATION(dst),
3537  uint src0_stride_z,
3538  uint src1_stride_z,
3539  uint dst_stride_z
3540 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3541  ,
3542  uint cross_plane_pad
3543 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
3544  )
3545 {
3546  int x = get_global_id(0) / MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
3547  int y = get_global_id(1) / MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;
3548  int z = get_global_id(2);
3549 
3550  // Offset
3551  const int offset_row_a = (get_global_id(1) % MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT) * 4;
3552  const int offset_row_b = (get_global_id(0) % MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH) * 8;
3553 
3554  // src_addr_a = address of matrix A
3555  // src_addr_b = address of matrix B
3556  int src0_addr_in_bytes = z * src0_stride_z + y * src0_stride_y + src0_offset_first_element_in_bytes;
3557  int src1_addr_in_bytes = x * src1_stride_y + src1_offset_first_element_in_bytes;
3558 
3559 #if defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
3560  // Do not slide matrix B if the matrix B has 3 dimensions and matrix A more than 3
3561  src1_addr_in_bytes += (z % MATRIX_B_DEPTH) * src1_stride_z;
3562 #else // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
3563  src1_addr_in_bytes += z * src1_stride_z;
3564 #endif // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
3565 
3566  __global half *src_addr_a = (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src0_addr_in_bytes);
3567  __global half *src_addr_b = (__global half *)(src1_ptr + src1_addr_in_bytes);
3568 
3569  // Compute end row address for matrix B
3570  __global half *src_end_addr_b = src_addr_b + COLS_B;
3571 
3572  src_addr_a += offset_row_a;
3573  src_addr_b += offset_row_b;
3574 
3575  // Reset accumulators
3576  half8 c00 = 0.0f;
3577  half8 c10 = 0.0f;
3578  half8 c20 = 0.0f;
3579  half8 c30 = 0.0f;
3580 
3581  for(; src_addr_b <= (src_end_addr_b - (int)(16 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH)); src_addr_a += 8 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT, src_addr_b += 16 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH)
3582  {
3583  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
3584  half4 a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a);
3585  half8 b0 = vload8(0, src_addr_b);
3586 
3587  c00 += (half8)a0.s0 * b0;
3588  c10 += (half8)a0.s1 * b0;
3589  c20 += (half8)a0.s2 * b0;
3590  c30 += (half8)a0.s3 * b0;
3591 
3592  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
3593  a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a + 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT);
3594  b0 = vload8(0, src_addr_b + 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH);
3595 
3596  c00 += (half8)a0.s0 * b0;
3597  c10 += (half8)a0.s1 * b0;
3598  c20 += (half8)a0.s2 * b0;
3599  c30 += (half8)a0.s3 * b0;
3600  }
3601 
3602  for(; src_addr_b < src_end_addr_b; src_addr_a += 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT, src_addr_b += 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH)
3603  {
3604  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
3605  half4 a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a);
3606  half8 b0 = vload8(0, src_addr_b);
3607 
3608  c00 += (half8)a0.s0 * b0;
3609  c10 += (half8)a0.s1 * b0;
3610  c20 += (half8)a0.s2 * b0;
3611  c30 += (half8)a0.s3 * b0;
3612  }
3613 
3614  // Compute destination address
3615  Image dst = CONVERT_TO_IMAGE_STRUCT(dst);
3616 
3617 #if defined(ALPHA)
3618  // Multiply by the weight of matrix product
3619  c00 = c00 * (half8)ALPHA;
3620  c10 = c10 * (half8)ALPHA;
3621  c20 = c20 * (half8)ALPHA;
3622  c30 = c30 * (half8)ALPHA;
3623 #endif // defined(ALPHA)
3624 
3625 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
3626  // *INDENT-OFF*
3627  // clang-format off
3628  __global half *src2_addr = (__global half *)(src2_ptr + src2_offset_first_element_in_bytes + get_global_id(0) * src2_step_x);
3629  half8 c0 = vload8(0, src2_addr);
3630  // clang-format on
3631  // *INDENT-ON*
3632 
3633  c00 += c0;
3634  c10 += c0;
3635  c20 += c0;
3636  c30 += c0;
3637 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
3638 
3639  // Compute dst address
3640  __global uchar *dst_addr = offset(&dst, 0, 0);
3641 
3642 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3643  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
3644  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
3645  //
3646  // | |
3647  // | plane0 |
3648  // | |
3649  // |__________________|
3650  // |******************|
3651  // | cross_plane_pad |
3652  // |******************|
3653  // | |
3654  // | plane1 |
3655  // | |
3656  // |__________________|
3657 
3658  // The plane (zout) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * 4) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
3659  uint4 zout = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * 4)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
3660  zout = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zout);
3661 
3662  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
3663  zout *= (cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
3664 
3665  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
3666  // multiply dst_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
3667  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
3668 
3669  // Store 4x8 block
3670  vstore8(c00, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y + zout.s0));
3671  vstore8(c10, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y + zout.s1));
3672  vstore8(c20, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y + zout.s2));
3673  vstore8(c30, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y + zout.s3));
3674 
3675 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3676  // Add offset for batched GEMM
3677  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z;
3678 
3679  // Store 4x8 block
3680  vstore8(c00, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y));
3681  vstore8(c10, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y));
3682  vstore8(c20, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y));
3683  vstore8(c30, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y));
3684 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3685 }

3733 __kernel void gemm_mm_interleaved_transposed_f16_acc32(IMAGE_DECLARATION(src0),
3734  IMAGE_DECLARATION(src1),
3735 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
3736  VECTOR_DECLARATION(src2),
3737 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
3738  IMAGE_DECLARATION(dst),
3739  uint src0_stride_z,
3740  uint src1_stride_z,
3741  uint dst_stride_z
3742 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3743  ,
3744  uint cross_plane_pad
3745 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
3746  )
3747 {
3748  int x = get_global_id(0) / MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
3749  int y = get_global_id(1) / MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;

3751

3753  const int offset_row_a = (get_global_id(1) % MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT) * 4;
3754  const int offset_row_b = (get_global_id(0) % MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH) * 8;
3755 
3756  // src_addr_a = address of matrix A
3757  // src_addr_b = address of matrix B
3758  int src0_addr_in_bytes = z * src0_stride_z + y * src0_stride_y + src0_offset_first_element_in_bytes;
3759  int src1_addr_in_bytes = x * src1_stride_y + src1_offset_first_element_in_bytes;
3760 
3761 #if defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
3762  // Do not slide matrix B if the matrix B has 3 dimensions and matrix A more than 3
3763  src1_addr_in_bytes += (z % MATRIX_B_DEPTH) * src1_stride_z;
3764 #else // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
3765  src1_addr_in_bytes += z * src1_stride_z;
3766 #endif // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)

3769  __global half *src_addr_b = (__global half *)(src1_ptr + src1_addr_in_bytes);
3770

3772  __global half *src_end_addr_b = src_addr_b + COLS_B;
3773

3775  src_addr_b += offset_row_b;
3776 
3777  // Reset accumulators
3778  float8 c00 = 0.0f;
3779  float8 c10 = 0.0f;
3780  float8 c20 = 0.0f;
3781  float8 c30 = 0.0f;
3782

3784  {
3785  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
3786  float4 a0 = convert_float4(vload4(0, src_addr_a));
3787  float8 b0 = convert_float8(vload8(0, src_addr_b));
3788 
3789  c00 += (float8)a0.s0 * b0;
3790  c10 += (float8)a0.s1 * b0;
3791  c20 += (float8)a0.s2 * b0;
3792  c30 += (float8)a0.s3 * b0;
3793 
3794  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
3795  a0 = convert_float4(vload4(0, src_addr_a + 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT));
3796  b0 = convert_float8(vload8(0, src_addr_b + 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH));
3797 
3798  c00 += (float8)a0.s0 * b0;
3799  c10 += (float8)a0.s1 * b0;
3800  c20 += (float8)a0.s2 * b0;
3801  c30 += (float8)a0.s3 * b0;
3802  }
3803 
3804  for(; src_addr_b < src_end_addr_b; src_addr_a += 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT, src_addr_b += 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH)
3805  {
3806  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)

3823  c20 = c20 * (float8)ALPHA;
3824  c30 = c30 * (float8)ALPHA;
3825 #endif // defined(ALPHA)

3830  __global half *src2_addr = (__global half *)(src2_ptr + src2_offset_first_element_in_bytes + get_global_id(0) * src2_step_x);

3843 
3844 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3845  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
3846  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
3847  //
3848  // | |

3851  // |__________________|
3852  // |******************|
3853  // | cross_plane_pad |
3854  // |******************|
3855  // | |
3856  // | plane1 |
3857  // | |
3858  // |__________________|
3859 
3860  // The plane (zout) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * 4) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
3861  uint4 zout = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * 4)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
3862  zout = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zout);
3863 
3864  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
3865  zout *= (cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
3866 
3867  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
