3868  // multiply dst_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
3869  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
3870 
3871  // Store 4x8 block
3872  vstore8(convert_half8(c00), 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y + zout.s0));
3873  vstore8(convert_half8(c10), 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y + zout.s1));
3874  vstore8(convert_half8(c20), 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y + zout.s2));
3875  vstore8(convert_half8(c30), 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y + zout.s3));
3876 
3877 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3878  // Add offset for batched GEMM
3879  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z;
3880 
3881  // Store 4x8 block
3882  vstore8(convert_half8(c00), 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y));
3883  vstore8(convert_half8(c10), 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y));
3884  vstore8(convert_half8(c20), 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y));
3885  vstore8(convert_half8(c30), 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y));
3886 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3887 }
3888 
3932 __kernel void gemm_mm_interleaved_transposed_f16_bifrost(IMAGE_DECLARATION(src0),
3933  IMAGE_DECLARATION(src1),
3934 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
3935  VECTOR_DECLARATION(src2),
3936 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
3937  IMAGE_DECLARATION(dst),
3938  uint src0_stride_z,
3939  uint src1_stride_z,
3940  uint dst_stride_z
3941 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
3942  ,
3943  uint cross_plane_pad
3944 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
3945  )
3946 {
3947  int x = get_global_id(0) / MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
3948  int y = get_global_id(1) / MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;
3949  int z = get_global_id(2);
3950 
3951  // Offset
3952  const int offset_row_a = (get_global_id(1) % MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT) * 4;
3953  const int offset_row_b = (get_global_id(0) % MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH) * 8;
3954 
3955  // src_addr_a = address of matrix A
3956  // src_addr_b = address of matrix B
3957  int src0_addr_in_bytes = z * src0_stride_z + y * src0_stride_y + src0_offset_first_element_in_bytes;
3958  int src1_addr_in_bytes = x * src1_stride_y + src1_offset_first_element_in_bytes;
3959 
3960 #if defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
3961  // Do not slide matrix B if the matrix B has 3 dimensions and matrix A more than 3
3962  src1_addr_in_bytes += (z % MATRIX_B_DEPTH) * src1_stride_z;
3963 #else // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
3964  src1_addr_in_bytes += z * src1_stride_z;
3965 #endif // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
3966 
3967  __global half *src_addr_a = (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src0_addr_in_bytes);
3968  __global half *src_addr_b = (__global half *)(src1_ptr + src1_addr_in_bytes);
3969 
3970  // Compute end row address for matrix B
3971  __global half *src_end_addr_b = src_addr_b + COLS_B;
3972 
3973  src_addr_a += offset_row_a;
3974  src_addr_b += offset_row_b;
3975 
3976  // Reset accumulators
3977  half8 c00 = 0.0f;
3978  half8 c10 = 0.0f;
3979  half8 c20 = 0.0f;
3980  half8 c30 = 0.0f;
3981 
3982 #define COLS_MTX_B (COLS_B / (8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH))
3983 
3984  int i = 0;
3985  for(; i <= (int)(COLS_MTX_B - 4); i += 4)
3986  {
3987 #if MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT == 1
3988  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
3989  half8 a0 = vload8(0, src_addr_a);
3990  half8 b0 = vload8(0, src_addr_b);
3991 
3992  src_addr_a += 8 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;
3993  src_addr_b += 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
3994 
3995  c00 = fma((half8)a0.s0, b0, c00);
3996  c10 = fma((half8)a0.s1, b0, c10);
3997  c20 = fma((half8)a0.s2, b0, c20);
3998  c30 = fma((half8)a0.s3, b0, c30);
3999 
4000  // Load values from matrix B (transposed)
4001  b0 = vload8(0, src_addr_b);
4002 
4003  src_addr_b += 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
4004 
4005  c00 = fma((half8)a0.s4, b0, c00);
4006  c10 = fma((half8)a0.s5, b0, c10);
4007  c20 = fma((half8)a0.s6, b0, c20);
4008  c30 = fma((half8)a0.s7, b0, c30);
4009 
4010  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
4011  a0 = vload8(0, src_addr_a);
4012  b0 = vload8(0, src_addr_b);
4013 
4014  src_addr_a += 8 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;
4015  src_addr_b += 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
4016 
4017  c00 = fma((half8)a0.s0, b0, c00);
4018  c10 = fma((half8)a0.s1, b0, c10);
4019  c20 = fma((half8)a0.s2, b0, c20);
4020  c30 = fma((half8)a0.s3, b0, c30);
4021 
4022  // Load values from matrix B (transposed)
4023  b0 = vload8(0, src_addr_b);
4024 
4025  src_addr_b += 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
4026 
4027  c00 = fma((half8)a0.s4, b0, c00);
4028  c10 = fma((half8)a0.s5, b0, c10);
4029  c20 = fma((half8)a0.s6, b0, c20);
4030  c30 = fma((half8)a0.s7, b0, c30);
4031 #else // MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT == 1
4032  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
4033  half4 a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a);
4034  half8 b0 = vload8(0, src_addr_b);
4035 
4036  src_addr_a += 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;
4037  src_addr_b += 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
4038 
4039  c00 = fma((half8)a0.s0, b0, c00);
4040  c10 = fma((half8)a0.s1, b0, c10);
4041  c20 = fma((half8)a0.s2, b0, c20);
4042  c30 = fma((half8)a0.s3, b0, c30);
4043 
4044  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
4045  a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a);
4046  b0 = vload8(0, src_addr_b);
4047 
4048  src_addr_a += 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;
4049  src_addr_b += 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
4050 
4051  c00 = fma((half8)a0.s0, b0, c00);
4052  c10 = fma((half8)a0.s1, b0, c10);
4053  c20 = fma((half8)a0.s2, b0, c20);
4054  c30 = fma((half8)a0.s3, b0, c30);
4055 
4056  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
4057  a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a);
4058  b0 = vload8(0, src_addr_b);
4059 
4060  src_addr_a += 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;
4061  src_addr_b += 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
4062 
4063  c00 = fma((half8)a0.s0, b0, c00);
4064  c10 = fma((half8)a0.s1, b0, c10);
4065  c20 = fma((half8)a0.s2, b0, c20);
4066  c30 = fma((half8)a0.s3, b0, c30);
4067 
4068  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
4069  a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a);
4070  b0 = vload8(0, src_addr_b);
4071 
4072  src_addr_a += 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;
4073  src_addr_b += 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
4074 
4075  c00 = fma((half8)a0.s0, b0, c00);
4076  c10 = fma((half8)a0.s1, b0, c10);
4077  c20 = fma((half8)a0.s2, b0, c20);
4078  c30 = fma((half8)a0.s3, b0, c30);
4079 #endif // MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT == 1
4080  }
4081 
4082  for(; i < (int)(COLS_MTX_B); ++i)
4083  {
4084  // Load values from matrix A (interleaved) and matrix B (transposed)
4085  half4 a0 = vload4(0, src_addr_a);
4086  half8 b0 = vload8(0, src_addr_b);
4087 
4088  src_addr_a += 4 * MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT;
4089  src_addr_b += 8 * MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH;
4090 
4091  c00 = fma((half8)a0.s0, b0, c00);
4092  c10 = fma((half8)a0.s1, b0, c10);
4093  c20 = fma((half8)a0.s2, b0, c20);
4094  c30 = fma((half8)a0.s3, b0, c30);
4095  }
4096 
4097  // Compute destination address
4098  Image dst = CONVERT_TO_IMAGE_STRUCT(dst);
4099 
4100 #if defined(ALPHA)
4101  // Multiply by the weight of matrix product
4102  c00 = c00 * (half8)ALPHA;
4103  c10 = c10 * (half8)ALPHA;
4104  c20 = c20 * (half8)ALPHA;
4105  c30 = c30 * (half8)ALPHA;
4106 #endif // defined(ALPHA)
4107 
4108 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
4109  // *INDENT-OFF*
4110  // clang-format off
4111  __global half *src2_addr = (__global half *)(src2_ptr + src2_offset_first_element_in_bytes + get_global_id(0) * src2_step_x);
4112  half8 c0 = vload8(0, src2_addr);
4113  // clang-format on
4114  // *INDENT-ON*
4115 
4116  c00 += c0;
4117  c10 += c0;
4118  c20 += c0;
4119  c30 += c0;
4120 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
4121 
4122  // Compute dst address
4123  __global uchar *dst_addr = offset(&dst, 0, 0);
4124 
4125 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
4126  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
4127  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
4128  //
4129  // | |
4130  // | plane0 |
4131  // | |
4132  // |__________________|
4133  // |******************|
4134  // | cross_plane_pad |
4135  // |******************|
4136  // | |
4137  // | plane1 |
4138  // | |
4139  // |__________________|
4140 
4141  // The plane (zout) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * 4) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
4142  uint4 zout = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * 4)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
4143  zout = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zout);
4144 
4145  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
4146  zout *= (cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
4147 
4148  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
4149  // multiply dst_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
4150  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
4151 
4152  // Store 4x8 block
4153  vstore8(c00, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y + zout.s0));
4154  vstore8(c10, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y + zout.s1));
4155  vstore8(c20, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y + zout.s2));
4156  vstore8(c30, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y + zout.s3));
4157 
4158 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
4159  // Add offset for batched GEMM
4160  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z;
4161 
4162  // Store 4x8 block
4163  vstore8(c00, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y));
4164  vstore8(c10, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y));
4165  vstore8(c20, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y));
4166  vstore8(c30, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y));
4167 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
4168 }
4169 
4170 // Undefine local defines
4171 #undef COLS_MTX_B
4172 
4173 #endif // defined(ARM_COMPUTE_OPENCL_FP16_ENABLED)
4174 
4175 #endif // defined(COLS_B) && defined(MULT_TRANSPOSE1XW_WIDTH) && defined(MULT_INTERLEAVE4X4_HEIGHT)
4176 
4177 #if defined(COLS_A) && defined(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X) && (NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y)
4178 #if defined(DATA_TYPE)
4179 #define VECTOR_TYPE VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X)
4180 
4228 __kernel void gemm_mm_floating_point(IMAGE_DECLARATION(src0),
4229  IMAGE_DECLARATION(src1),
4230 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
4231  VECTOR_DECLARATION(src2),
4232 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
4233  IMAGE_DECLARATION(dst),
4234  uint src0_stride_z,
4235  uint src1_stride_z,
4236  uint dst_stride_z
4237 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4238  ,
4239  uint src_cross_plane_pad
4240 #endif // REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D
4241 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
4242  ,
4243  uint dst_cross_plane_pad
4244 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
4245  )
4246 {
4247  int idx = get_global_id(0) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X;
4248 
4249  // Compute starting address for matrix A and Matrix B
4250  int2 src_addr = ((int2)(src0_offset_first_element_in_bytes, src1_offset_first_element_in_bytes));
4251 
4252  // Update address for the matrix A
4253  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(1) * src0_stride_y * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y;
4254 
4255  // Update address for the matrix B
4256  src_addr.s1 += idx * sizeof(DATA_TYPE);
4257 
4258 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4259  // Since we load a 2D input tile from a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
4260  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
4261  //
4262  // | |
4263  // | plane0 |
4264  // | |
4265  // |__________________|
4266  // |******************|
4267  // | cross_plane_pad |
4268  // |******************|
4269  // | |
4270  // | plane1 |
4271  // | |
4272  // |__________________|
4273 
4274  // The plane (zin) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
4275  uint4 zin = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
4276  zin = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zin);
4277 
4278  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
4279  zin *= (src_cross_plane_pad * src0_stride_y);
4280 
4281  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
4282  // multiply src0_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
4283  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(2) * src0_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
4284 
4285 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4286 
4287  // Add offset for batched GEMM
4288  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(2) * src0_stride_z;
4289 
4290 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4291 
4292 #if defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
4293  // Do not slide matrix B if the matrix B has 3 dimensions and matrix A more than 3
4294  src_addr.s1 += (get_global_id(2) % MATRIX_B_DEPTH) * src1_stride_z;
4295 #else // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
4296  src_addr.s1 += get_global_id(2) * src1_stride_z;
4297 #endif // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
4298 
4299  int end_row_vec_a = src_addr.s0 + (COLS_A * sizeof(DATA_TYPE));
4300 
4301  VECTOR_TYPE acc0 = 0.0f;
4302 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4303  VECTOR_TYPE acc1 = 0.0f;
4304 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4305 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4306  VECTOR_TYPE acc2 = 0.0f;
4307 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4308 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4309  VECTOR_TYPE acc3 = 0.0f;
4310 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4311 
4312  for(; src_addr.s0 <= (end_row_vec_a - 2 * (int)sizeof(DATA_TYPE)); src_addr += (int2)(2 * sizeof(DATA_TYPE), 2 * src1_stride_y))
4313  {
4314 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4315  // Load values from matrix A
4316  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
4317  a0 = vload2(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y + zin.s0));
4318 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4319  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
4320  a1 = vload2(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y + zin.s1));
4321 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4322 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4323  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
4324  a2 = vload2(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y + zin.s2));
4325 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4326 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4327  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
4328  a3 = vload2(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y + zin.s3));
4329 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4330 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4331  // Load values from matrix A
4332  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
4333  a0 = vload2(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y));
4334 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4335  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
4336  a1 = vload2(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y));
4337 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4338 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4339  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
4340  a2 = vload2(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y));
4341 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4342 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4343  VEC_DATA_TYPE(DATA_TYPE, 2)
4344  a3 = vload2(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y));
4345 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4346 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4347 
4348  // Load values from matrix B
4349  VECTOR_TYPE b0 = VLOAD(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
4350  VECTOR_TYPE b1 = VLOAD(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1 + src1_stride_y));
4351 
4352  // Accumulate
4353  acc0 += b0 * (VECTOR_TYPE)a0.s0;
4354  acc0 += b1 * (VECTOR_TYPE)a0.s1;
4355 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4356  acc1 += b0 * (VECTOR_TYPE)a1.s0;
4357  acc1 += b1 * (VECTOR_TYPE)a1.s1;
4358 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4359 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4360  acc2 += b0 * (VECTOR_TYPE)a2.s0;
4361  acc2 += b1 * (VECTOR_TYPE)a2.s1;
4362 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4363 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4364  acc3 += b0 * (VECTOR_TYPE)a3.s0;
4365  acc3 += b1 * (VECTOR_TYPE)a3.s1;
4366 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4367  }
4368 
4369  for(; src_addr.s0 < end_row_vec_a; src_addr += (int2)(sizeof(DATA_TYPE), src1_stride_y))
4370  {
4371 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4372  // Load values from matrix A
4373  DATA_TYPE a0 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y + zin.s0));
4374 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4375  DATA_TYPE a1 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y + zin.s1));
4376 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4377 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4378  DATA_TYPE a2 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y + zin.s2));
4379 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4380 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4381  DATA_TYPE a3 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y + zin.s3));
4382 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4383 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4384  // Load values from matrix A
4385  DATA_TYPE a0 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y));
4386 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4387  DATA_TYPE a1 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y));
4388 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4389 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4390  DATA_TYPE a2 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y));
4391 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4392 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4393  DATA_TYPE a3 = *((__global DATA_TYPE *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y));
4394 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4395 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4396 
4397  // Load values from matrix B
4398  VECTOR_TYPE b0 = VLOAD(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X)(0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
4399 
4400  // Accumulate
4401  acc0 += b0 * (VECTOR_TYPE)a0;
4402 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4403  acc1 += b0 * (VECTOR_TYPE)a1;
4404 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4405 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4406  acc2 += b0 * (VECTOR_TYPE)a2;
4407 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4408 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4409  acc3 += b0 * (VECTOR_TYPE)a3;
4410 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4411  }
4412 
4413  // Compute destination address
4414  Image dst = CONVERT_TO_IMAGE_STRUCT(dst);
4415 
4416  // Compute dst address
4417  __global uchar *dst_addr = offset(&dst, 0, 0);
4418 
4419  // Multiply by the weight of matrix-matrix product and store the result
4420 #if defined(ALPHA)
4421  acc0 = acc0 * (VECTOR_TYPE)ALPHA;
4422 #endif // defined(ALPHA)
4423 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1 && defined(ALPHA)
4424  acc1 = acc1 * (VECTOR_TYPE)ALPHA;
4425 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1 && defined(ALPHA)
4426 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2 && defined(ALPHA)
4427  acc2 = acc2 * (VECTOR_TYPE)ALPHA;
4428 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2 && defined(ALPHA)
4429 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3 && defined(ALPHA)
4430  acc3 = acc3 * (VECTOR_TYPE)ALPHA;
4431 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3 && defined(ALPHA)
4432 
4433 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
4434  // *INDENT-OFF*
4435  // clang-format off
4436  __global DATA_TYPE *src2_addr = (__global DATA_TYPE *)(src2_ptr + src2_offset_first_element_in_bytes + get_global_id(0) * src2_step_x);
4437  VECTOR_TYPE c0 = VLOAD(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X)(0, src2_addr);
4438  // clang-format on
4439  // *INDENT-ON*
4440 
4441  acc0 += c0;
4442 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4443  acc1 += c0;
4444 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4445 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4446  acc2 += c0;
4447 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4448 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4449  acc3 += c0;
4450 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4451 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
4452 
4453  int z = get_global_id(2);
4454 
4455 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
4456  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
4457  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
4458  //
4459  // | |
4460  // | plane0 |
4461  // | |
4462  // |__________________|
4463  // |******************|
4464  // | cross_plane_pad |
4465  // |******************|
4466  // | |
4467  // | plane1 |
4468  // | |
4469  // |__________________|
4470 
4471  // The plane (zout) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
4472  uint4 zout = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
4473  zout = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zout);
4474 
4475  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
4476  zout *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
4477 
4478  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
4479  // multiply dst_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
4480  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
4481 
4482  // Store output block
4483  VSTORE(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X)
4484  (acc0, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y + zout.s0));
4485 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4486  VSTORE(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X)
4487  (acc1, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y + zout.s1));
4488 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4489 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4490  VSTORE(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X)
4491  (acc2, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y + zout.s2));
4492 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4493 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4494  VSTORE(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X)
4495  (acc3, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y + zout.s3));
4496 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4497 
4498 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
4499  // Add offset for batched GEMM
4500  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z;
4501 
4502  // Store output block
4503  VSTORE(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X)
4504  (acc0, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y));
4505 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4506  VSTORE(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X)
4507  (acc1, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y));
4508 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4509 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4510  VSTORE(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X)
4511  (acc2, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y));
4512 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4513 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4514  VSTORE(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X)
4515  (acc3, 0, (__global DATA_TYPE *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y));
4516 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4517 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
4518 }
4519 #endif // defined(DATA_TYPE)
4520 
4570 __kernel void gemm_mm_floating_point_f32_bifrost(IMAGE_DECLARATION(src0),
4571  IMAGE_DECLARATION(src1),
4572 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
4573  VECTOR_DECLARATION(src2),
4574 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
4575  IMAGE_DECLARATION(dst),
4576  uint src0_stride_z,
4577  uint src1_stride_z,
4578  uint dst_stride_z
4579 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4580  ,
4581  uint src_cross_plane_pad
4582 #endif // REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D
4583 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
4584  ,
4585  uint dst_cross_plane_pad
4586 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
4587  )
4588 {
4589  int idx = get_global_id(0) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X;
4590 
4591  // Compute starting address for matrix A and matrix B
4592  int2 src_addr = ((int2)(src0_offset_first_element_in_bytes, src1_offset_first_element_in_bytes));
4593 
4594  // Update address for matrix A
4595  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(1) * src0_stride_y * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y;
4596 
4597  // Update address for matrix B
4598  src_addr.s1 += idx * sizeof(float);
4599 
4600 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4601  // Since we load a 2D input tile from a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
4602  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
4603  //
4604  // | |
4605  // | plane0 |
4606  // | |
4607  // |__________________|
4608  // |******************|
4609  // | cross_plane_pad |
4610  // |******************|
4611  // | |
4612  // | plane1 |
4613  // | |
4614  // |__________________|
4615 
4616  // The plane (zin) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
4617  uint4 zin = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
4618  zin = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zin);
4619 
4620  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
4621  zin *= (src_cross_plane_pad * src0_stride_y);
4622 
4623  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
4624  // multiply src0_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
4625  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(2) * src0_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
4626 
4627 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4628 
4629  // Add offset for batched GEMM
4630  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(2) * src0_stride_z;
4631 
4632 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4633 
4634 #if defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
4635  // Do not slide matrix B if the matrix B has 3 dimensions and matrix A more than 3
4636  src_addr.s1 += (get_global_id(2) % MATRIX_B_DEPTH) * src1_stride_z;
4637 #else // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
4638  src_addr.s1 += get_global_id(2) * src1_stride_z;
4639 #endif // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
4640 
4641  // Initialize accumulators
4642  float acc00 = 0.0f;
4643  float acc01 = 0.0f;
4644  float acc02 = 0.0f;
4645  float acc03 = 0.0f;
4646 
4647 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4648  float acc10 = 0.0f;
4649  float acc11 = 0.0f;
4650  float acc12 = 0.0f;
4651  float acc13 = 0.0f;
4652 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4653 
4654 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4655  float acc20 = 0.0f;
4656  float acc21 = 0.0f;
4657  float acc22 = 0.0f;
4658  float acc23 = 0.0f;
4659 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4660 
4661 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4662  float acc30 = 0.0f;
4663  float acc31 = 0.0f;
4664  float acc32 = 0.0f;
4665  float acc33 = 0.0f;
4666 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4667 
4668  // A and B src indices get incremented at the same time.
4669  int i = 0;
4670  for(; i <= ((int)COLS_A - 4); i += 4)
4671  {
4672 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4673  // Load values from matrix A and matrix B
4674  float4 a0 = vload4(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y + zin.s0));
4675 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4676  float4 a1 = vload4(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y + zin.s1));
4677 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4678 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4679  float4 a2 = vload4(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y + zin.s2));
4680 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4681 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4682  float4 a3 = vload4(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y + zin.s3));
4683 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4684 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4685  // Load values from matrix A and matrix B
4686  float4 a0 = vload4(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y));
4687 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4688  float4 a1 = vload4(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y));
4689 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4690 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4691  float4 a2 = vload4(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y));
4692 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4693 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4694  float4 a3 = vload4(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y));
4695 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4696 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4697 
4698  float4 b0 = vload4(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
4699  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
4700 
4701  // Multiply and accumulate
4702  acc00 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s0, acc00);
4703  acc01 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s1, acc01);
4704  acc02 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s2, acc02);
4705  acc03 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s3, acc03);
4706 
4707 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4708 
4709  acc10 = fma(a1.s0, b0.s0, acc10);
4710  acc11 = fma(a1.s0, b0.s1, acc11);
4711  acc12 = fma(a1.s0, b0.s2, acc12);
4712  acc13 = fma(a1.s0, b0.s3, acc13);
4713 
4714 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4715 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4716 
4717  acc20 = fma(a2.s0, b0.s0, acc20);
4718  acc21 = fma(a2.s0, b0.s1, acc21);
4719  acc22 = fma(a2.s0, b0.s2, acc22);
4720  acc23 = fma(a2.s0, b0.s3, acc23);
4721 
4722 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4723 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4724 
4725  acc30 = fma(a3.s0, b0.s0, acc30);
4726  acc31 = fma(a3.s0, b0.s1, acc31);
4727  acc32 = fma(a3.s0, b0.s2, acc32);
4728  acc33 = fma(a3.s0, b0.s3, acc33);
4729 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4730 
4731  // Load values from matrix A and matrix B
4732  b0 = vload4(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
4733  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
4734 
4735  // Multiply and accumulate
4736  acc00 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s0, acc00);
4737  acc01 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s1, acc01);
4738  acc02 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s2, acc02);
4739  acc03 = fma(a0.s1, b0.s3, acc03);
4740 
4741 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4742 
4743  acc10 = fma(a1.s1, b0.s0, acc10);
4744  acc11 = fma(a1.s1, b0.s1, acc11);
4745  acc12 = fma(a1.s1, b0.s2, acc12);
4746  acc13 = fma(a1.s1, b0.s3, acc13);
4747 
4748 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4749 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4750 
4751  acc20 = fma(a2.s1, b0.s0, acc20);
4752  acc21 = fma(a2.s1, b0.s1, acc21);
4753  acc22 = fma(a2.s1, b0.s2, acc22);
4754  acc23 = fma(a2.s1, b0.s3, acc23);
4755 
4756 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4757 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4758 
4759  acc30 = fma(a3.s1, b0.s0, acc30);
4760  acc31 = fma(a3.s1, b0.s1, acc31);
4761  acc32 = fma(a3.s1, b0.s2, acc32);
4762  acc33 = fma(a3.s1, b0.s3, acc33);
4763 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4764 
4765  // Load values from matrix A and matrix B
4766  b0 = vload4(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
4767  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
4768 
4769  // Multiply and accumulate
4770  acc00 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s0, acc00);
4771  acc01 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s1, acc01);
4772  acc02 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s2, acc02);
4773  acc03 = fma(a0.s2, b0.s3, acc03);
4774 
4775 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4776 
4777  acc10 = fma(a1.s2, b0.s0, acc10);
4778  acc11 = fma(a1.s2, b0.s1, acc11);
4779  acc12 = fma(a1.s2, b0.s2, acc12);
4780  acc13 = fma(a1.s2, b0.s3, acc13);
4781 
4782 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4783 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4784 
4785  acc20 = fma(a2.s2, b0.s0, acc20);
4786  acc21 = fma(a2.s2, b0.s1, acc21);
4787  acc22 = fma(a2.s2, b0.s2, acc22);
4788  acc23 = fma(a2.s2, b0.s3, acc23);
4789 
4790 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4791 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4792 
4793  acc30 = fma(a3.s2, b0.s0, acc30);
4794  acc31 = fma(a3.s2, b0.s1, acc31);
4795  acc32 = fma(a3.s2, b0.s2, acc32);
4796  acc33 = fma(a3.s2, b0.s3, acc33);
4797 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4798 
4799  // Load values from matrix A and matrix B
4800  b0 = vload4(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
4801  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
4802 
4803  // Multiply and accumulate
4804  acc00 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s0, acc00);
4805  acc01 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s1, acc01);
4806  acc02 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s2, acc02);
4807  acc03 = fma(a0.s3, b0.s3, acc03);
4808 
4809 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4810 
4811  acc10 = fma(a1.s3, b0.s0, acc10);
4812  acc11 = fma(a1.s3, b0.s1, acc11);
4813  acc12 = fma(a1.s3, b0.s2, acc12);
4814  acc13 = fma(a1.s3, b0.s3, acc13);
4815 
4816 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4817 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4818 
4819  acc20 = fma(a2.s3, b0.s0, acc20);
4820  acc21 = fma(a2.s3, b0.s1, acc21);
4821  acc22 = fma(a2.s3, b0.s2, acc22);
4822  acc23 = fma(a2.s3, b0.s3, acc23);
4823 
4824 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4825 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4826 
4827  acc30 = fma(a3.s3, b0.s0, acc30);
4828  acc31 = fma(a3.s3, b0.s1, acc31);
4829  acc32 = fma(a3.s3, b0.s2, acc32);
4830  acc33 = fma(a3.s3, b0.s3, acc33);
4831 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4832 
4833  src_addr.s0 += 4 * sizeof(float);
4834  }
4835 
4836  for(; i < (int)COLS_A; ++i)
4837  {
4838 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4839  // Load values from matrix A
4840  float a0 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y + zin.s0));
4841 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4842  float a1 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y + zin.s1));
4843 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4844 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4845  float a2 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y + zin.s2));
4846 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4847 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4848  float a3 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y + zin.s3));
4849 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4850 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4851  // Load values from matrix A
4852  float a0 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y));
4853 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4854  float a1 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y));
4855 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4856 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4857  float a2 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y));
4858 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4859 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4860  float a3 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y));
4861 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4862 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
4863 
4864  // Load values from matrix B
4865  float4 b0 = vload4(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
4866  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
4867 
4868  // Multiply and accumulate
4869  acc00 = fma(a0, b0.s0, acc00);
4870  acc01 = fma(a0, b0.s1, acc01);
4871  acc02 = fma(a0, b0.s2, acc02);
4872  acc03 = fma(a0, b0.s3, acc03);
4873 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4874  acc10 = fma(a1, b0.s0, acc10);
4875  acc11 = fma(a1, b0.s1, acc11);
4876  acc12 = fma(a1, b0.s2, acc12);
4877  acc13 = fma(a1, b0.s3, acc13);
4878 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4879 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4880  acc20 = fma(a2, b0.s0, acc20);
4881  acc21 = fma(a2, b0.s1, acc21);
4882  acc22 = fma(a2, b0.s2, acc22);
4883  acc23 = fma(a2, b0.s3, acc23);
4884 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4885 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4886  acc30 = fma(a3, b0.s0, acc30);
4887  acc31 = fma(a3, b0.s1, acc31);
4888  acc32 = fma(a3, b0.s2, acc32);
4889  acc33 = fma(a3, b0.s3, acc33);
4890 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4891 
4892  src_addr.s0 += sizeof(float);
4893  }
4894 
4895  int z = get_global_id(2);
4896 
4897  // Compute destination address
4898  Image dst = CONVERT_TO_IMAGE_STRUCT(dst);
4899 
4900  // Multiply by the weight of matrix-matrix product and store the result
4901 #if defined(ALPHA)
4902  acc00 = acc00 * ALPHA;
4903  acc01 = acc01 * ALPHA;
4904  acc02 = acc02 * ALPHA;
4905  acc03 = acc03 * ALPHA;
4906 #endif // defined(ALPHA)
4907 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1 && defined(ALPHA)
4908  acc10 = acc10 * ALPHA;
4909  acc11 = acc11 * ALPHA;
4910  acc12 = acc12 * ALPHA;
4911  acc13 = acc13 * ALPHA;
4912 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1 && defined(ALPHA)
4913 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2 && defined(ALPHA)
4914  acc20 = acc20 * ALPHA;
4915  acc21 = acc21 * ALPHA;
4916  acc22 = acc22 * ALPHA;
4917  acc23 = acc23 * ALPHA;
4918 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2 && defined(ALPHA)
4919 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3 && defined(ALPHA)
4920  acc30 = acc30 * ALPHA;
4921  acc31 = acc31 * ALPHA;
4922  acc32 = acc32 * ALPHA;
4923  acc33 = acc33 * ALPHA;
4924 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3 && defined(ALPHA)
4925 
4926  // Compute dst address
4927  __global uchar *dst_addr = offset(&dst, 0, 0);
4928 
4929 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
4930  __global float *src2_addr = (__global float *)(src2_ptr + src2_offset_first_element_in_bytes + get_global_id(0) * src2_step_x);
4931  float4 c0 = vload4(0, src2_addr);
4932 
4933  acc00 += c0.s0;
4934  acc01 += c0.s1;
4935  acc02 += c0.s2;
4936  acc03 += c0.s3;
4937 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4938  acc10 += c0.s0;
4939  acc11 += c0.s1;
4940  acc12 += c0.s2;
4941  acc13 += c0.s3;
4942 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4943 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4944  acc20 += c0.s0;
4945  acc21 += c0.s1;
4946  acc22 += c0.s2;
4947  acc23 += c0.s3;
4948 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4949 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4950  acc30 += c0.s0;
4951  acc31 += c0.s1;
4952  acc32 += c0.s2;
4953  acc33 += c0.s3;
4954 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4955 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
4956 
4957 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
4958  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
4959  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
4960  //
4961  // | |
4962  // | plane0 |
4963  // | |
4964  // |__________________|
4965  // |******************|
4966  // | cross_plane_pad |
4967  // |******************|
4968  // | |
4969  // | plane1 |
4970  // | |
4971  // |__________________|
4972 
4973  // The plane (zout) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
4974  uint4 zout = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
4975  zout = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zout);
4976 
4977  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
4978  zout *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
4979 
4980  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
4981  // multiply dst_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
4982  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
4983 
4984  // Store the output block
4985  vstore4((float4)(acc00, acc01, acc02, acc03), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y + zout.s0));
4986 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4987  vstore4((float4)(acc10, acc11, acc12, acc13), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y + zout.s1));
4988 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
4989 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4990  vstore4((float4)(acc20, acc21, acc22, acc23), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y + zout.s2));
4991 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
4992 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4993  vstore4((float4)(acc30, acc31, acc32, acc33), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y + zout.s3));
4994 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
4995 
4996 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
4997  // Add offset for batched GEMM
4998  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z;
4999 
5000  // Store the output block
5001  vstore4((float4)(acc00, acc01, acc02, acc03), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y));
5002 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5003  vstore4((float4)(acc10, acc11, acc12, acc13), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y));
5004 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5005 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5006  vstore4((float4)(acc20, acc21, acc22, acc23), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y));
5007 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5008 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5009  vstore4((float4)(acc30, acc31, acc32, acc33), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y));
5010 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5011 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
5012 }
5013 
5064 __kernel void gemm_mm_floating_point_f32_bifrost_1000(IMAGE_DECLARATION(src0),
5065  IMAGE_DECLARATION(src1),
5066 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
5067  VECTOR_DECLARATION(src2),
5068 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
5069  IMAGE_DECLARATION(dst),
5070  uint src0_stride_z,
5071  uint src1_stride_z,
5072  uint dst_stride_z
5073 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5074  ,
5075  uint src_cross_plane_pad
5076 #endif // REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D
5077 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
5078  ,
5079  uint dst_cross_plane_pad
5080 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
5081  )
5082 {
5083  // Requires 2 NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X, C vect2, A vect4, B (2 vload2) // to fix for NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5084  int idx = get_global_id(0) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X;
5085 
5086  // Compute starting address for matrix A and Matrix B
5087  int2 src_addr = ((int2)(src0_offset_first_element_in_bytes, src1_offset_first_element_in_bytes));
5088 
5089  // Update address for the matrix A
5090  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(1) * src0_stride_y * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y;
5091 
5092  // Update address for the matrix B
5093  src_addr.s1 += idx * sizeof(float);
5094 
5095 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5096  // Since we load a 2D input tile from a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
5097  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
5098  //
5099  // | |
5100  // | plane0 |
5101  // | |
5102  // |__________________|
5103  // |******************|
5104  // | cross_plane_pad |
5105  // |******************|
5106  // | |
5107  // | plane1 |
5108  // | |
5109  // |__________________|
5110 
5111  // The plane (zin) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
5112  uint4 zin = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
5113  zin = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zin);
5114 
5115  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
5116  zin *= (src_cross_plane_pad * src0_stride_y);
5117 
5118  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
5119  // multiply src0_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
5120  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(2) * src0_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
5121 
5122 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5123 
5124  // Add offset for batched GEMM
5125  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(2) * src0_stride_z;
5126 
5127 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5128 
5129 #if defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
5130  // Do not slide matrix B if the matrix B has 3 dimensions and matrix A more than 3
5131  src_addr.s1 += (get_global_id(2) % MATRIX_B_DEPTH) * src1_stride_z;
5132 #else // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
5133  src_addr.s1 += get_global_id(2) * src1_stride_z;
5134 #endif // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
5135 
5136  // Initialize accumulators
5137  float acc00 = 0.0f;
5138  float acc01 = 0.0f;
5139 
5140 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5141  float acc10 = 0.0f;
5142  float acc11 = 0.0f;
5143 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5144 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5145  float acc20 = 0.0f;
5146  float acc21 = 0.0f;
5147 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5148 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5149  float acc30 = 0.0f;
5150  float acc31 = 0.0f;
5151 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5152 
5153  // A and B src indices get incremented at the same time.
5154  int i = 0;
5155  for(; i <= ((int)COLS_A - 8); i += 8)
5156  {
5157 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5158  // Load values from matrix A
5159  float8 a0 = vload8(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + zin.s0));
5160 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5161  // Load values from matrix A
5162  float8 a0 = vload8(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0));
5163 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5164 
5165  // Load values from matrix B
5166  float2 b0 = vload2(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
5167  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5168  float2 b1 = vload2(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
5169  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5170  float2 b2 = vload2(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
5171  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5172  float2 b3 = vload2(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
5173  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5174  float2 b4 = vload2(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
5175  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5176  float2 b5 = vload2(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
5177  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5178  float2 b6 = vload2(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
5179  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5180  float2 b7 = vload2(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
5181  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5182 
5183  // Multiply and accumulate
5184  acc00 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s0, acc00);
5185  acc00 = fma(a0.s1, b1.s0, acc00);
5186  acc00 = fma(a0.s2, b2.s0, acc00);
5187  acc00 = fma(a0.s3, b3.s0, acc00);
5188  acc00 = fma(a0.s4, b4.s0, acc00);
5189  acc00 = fma(a0.s5, b5.s0, acc00);
5190  acc00 = fma(a0.s6, b6.s0, acc00);
5191  acc00 = fma(a0.s7, b7.s0, acc00);
5192 
5193  acc01 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s1, acc01);
5194  acc01 = fma(a0.s1, b1.s1, acc01);
5195  acc01 = fma(a0.s2, b2.s1, acc01);
5196  acc01 = fma(a0.s3, b3.s1, acc01);
5197  acc01 = fma(a0.s4, b4.s1, acc01);
5198  acc01 = fma(a0.s5, b5.s1, acc01);
5199  acc01 = fma(a0.s6, b6.s1, acc01);
5200  acc01 = fma(a0.s7, b7.s1, acc01);
5201 
5202 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5203 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5204  a0 = vload8(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y + zin.s1));
5205 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5206  a0 = vload8(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y));
5207 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5208  acc10 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s0, acc10);
5209  acc10 = fma(a0.s1, b1.s0, acc10);
5210  acc10 = fma(a0.s2, b2.s0, acc10);
5211  acc10 = fma(a0.s3, b3.s0, acc10);
5212  acc10 = fma(a0.s4, b4.s0, acc10);
5213  acc10 = fma(a0.s5, b5.s0, acc10);
5214  acc10 = fma(a0.s6, b6.s0, acc10);
5215  acc10 = fma(a0.s7, b7.s0, acc10);
5216 
5217  acc11 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s1, acc11);
5218  acc11 = fma(a0.s1, b1.s1, acc11);
5219  acc11 = fma(a0.s2, b2.s1, acc11);
5220  acc11 = fma(a0.s3, b3.s1, acc11);
5221  acc11 = fma(a0.s4, b4.s1, acc11);
5222  acc11 = fma(a0.s5, b5.s1, acc11);
5223  acc11 = fma(a0.s6, b6.s1, acc11);
5224  acc11 = fma(a0.s7, b7.s1, acc11);
5225 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5226 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5227 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5228  a0 = vload8(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y + zin.s2));
5229 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5230  a0 = vload8(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y));
5231 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5232  acc20 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s0, acc20);
5233  acc20 = fma(a0.s1, b1.s0, acc20);
5234  acc20 = fma(a0.s2, b2.s0, acc20);
5235  acc20 = fma(a0.s3, b3.s0, acc20);
5236  acc20 = fma(a0.s4, b4.s0, acc20);
5237  acc20 = fma(a0.s5, b5.s0, acc20);
5238  acc20 = fma(a0.s6, b6.s0, acc20);
5239  acc20 = fma(a0.s7, b7.s0, acc20);
5240 
5241  acc21 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s1, acc21);
5242  acc21 = fma(a0.s1, b1.s1, acc21);
5243  acc21 = fma(a0.s2, b2.s1, acc21);
5244  acc21 = fma(a0.s3, b3.s1, acc21);
5245  acc21 = fma(a0.s4, b4.s1, acc21);
5246  acc21 = fma(a0.s5, b5.s1, acc21);
5247  acc21 = fma(a0.s6, b6.s1, acc21);
5248  acc21 = fma(a0.s7, b7.s1, acc21);
5249 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5250 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5251 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5252  a0 = vload8(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y + zin.s3));
5253 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5254  a0 = vload8(0, (__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y));
5255 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5256  acc30 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s0, acc30);
5257  acc30 = fma(a0.s1, b1.s0, acc30);
5258  acc30 = fma(a0.s2, b2.s0, acc30);
5259  acc30 = fma(a0.s3, b3.s0, acc30);
5260  acc30 = fma(a0.s4, b4.s0, acc30);
5261  acc30 = fma(a0.s5, b5.s0, acc30);
5262  acc30 = fma(a0.s6, b6.s0, acc30);
5263  acc30 = fma(a0.s7, b7.s0, acc30);
5264 
5265  acc31 = fma(a0.s0, b0.s1, acc31);
5266  acc31 = fma(a0.s1, b1.s1, acc31);
5267  acc31 = fma(a0.s2, b2.s1, acc31);
5268  acc31 = fma(a0.s3, b3.s1, acc31);
5269  acc31 = fma(a0.s4, b4.s1, acc31);
5270  acc31 = fma(a0.s5, b5.s1, acc31);
5271  acc31 = fma(a0.s6, b6.s1, acc31);
5272  acc31 = fma(a0.s7, b7.s1, acc31);
5273 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5274 
5275  src_addr.s0 += sizeof(float) * 8;
5276  }
5277  // float size increment
5278  for(; i < (int)COLS_A; ++i)
5279  {
5280 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5281  // Load values from matrix A
5282  float a0 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y + zin.s0));
5283 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5284  float a1 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y + zin.s1));
5285 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5286 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5287  float a2 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y + zin.s2));
5288 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5289 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5290  float a3 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y + zin.s3));
5291 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5292 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5293  // Load values from matrix A
5294  float a0 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y));
5295 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5296  float a1 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y));
5297 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5298 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5299  float a2 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y));
5300 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5301 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5302  float a3 = *((__global float *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y));
5303 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5304 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5305 
5306  // Load values from matrix B
5307  float2 b0 = vload2(0, (__global float *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
5308  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5309 
5310  // Multiply and accumulate
5311  acc00 = fma(a0, b0.s0, acc00);
5312  acc01 = fma(a0, b0.s1, acc01);
5313 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5314  acc10 = fma(a1, b0.s0, acc10);
5315  acc11 = fma(a1, b0.s1, acc11);
5316 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5317 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5318  acc20 = fma(a2, b0.s0, acc20);
5319  acc21 = fma(a2, b0.s1, acc21);
5320 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5321 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5322  acc30 = fma(a3, b0.s0, acc30);
5323  acc31 = fma(a3, b0.s1, acc31);
5324 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5325 
5326  src_addr.s0 += sizeof(float);
5327  }
5328 
5329  // Multiply by the weight of matrix-matrix product and store the result
5330 #if defined(ALPHA)
5331  acc00 = acc00 * ALPHA;
5332  acc01 = acc01 * ALPHA;
5333 #endif // defined(ALPHA)
5334 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1 && defined(ALPHA)
5335  acc10 = acc10 * ALPHA;
5336  acc11 = acc11 * ALPHA;
5337 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1 && defined(ALPHA)
5338 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2 && defined(ALPHA)
5339  acc20 = acc20 * ALPHA;
5340  acc21 = acc21 * ALPHA;
5341 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2 && defined(ALPHA)
5342 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3 && defined(ALPHA)
5343  acc30 = acc30 * ALPHA;
5344  acc31 = acc31 * ALPHA;
5345 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3 && defined(ALPHA)
5346 
5347  int z = get_global_id(2);
5348 
5349  // Compute destination address
5350  Image dst = CONVERT_TO_IMAGE_STRUCT(dst);
5351 
5352  // Compute dst address
5353  __global uchar *dst_addr = offset(&dst, 0, 0);
5354 
5355 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
5356  __global float *src2_addr = (__global float *)(src2_ptr + src2_offset_first_element_in_bytes + get_global_id(0) * src2_step_x);
5357  float2 c0 = vload2(0, src2_addr);
5358 
5359  acc00 += c0.s0;
5360  acc01 += c0.s1;
5361 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5362  acc10 += c0.s0;
5363  acc11 += c0.s1;
5364 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5365 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5366  acc20 += c0.s0;
5367  acc21 += c0.s1;
5368 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5369 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5370  acc30 += c0.s0;
5371  acc31 += c0.s1;
5372 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5373 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
5374 
5375 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
5376  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
5377  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
5378  //
5379  // | |
5380  // | plane0 |
5381  // | |
5382  // |__________________|
5383  // |******************|
5384  // | cross_plane_pad |
5385  // |******************|
5386  // | |
5387  // | plane1 |
5388  // | |
5389  // |__________________|
5390 
5391  // The plane (zout) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
5392  uint4 zout = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
5393  zout = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zout);
5394 
5395  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
5396  zout *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
5397 
5398  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
5399  // multiply dst_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
5400  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
5401 
5402  // Store the output block
5403  vstore2((float2)(acc00, acc01), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y + zout.s0));
5404 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5405  vstore2((float2)(acc10, acc11), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y + zout.s1));
5406 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5407 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5408  vstore2((float2)(acc20, acc21), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y + zout.s2));
5409 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5410 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5411  vstore2((float2)(acc30, acc31), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y + zout.s3));
5412 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5413 
5414 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
5415  // Add offset for batched GEMM
5416  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z;
5417 
5418  // Store the output block
5419  vstore2((float2)(acc00, acc01), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y));
5420 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5421  vstore2((float2)(acc10, acc11), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y));
5422 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5423 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5424  vstore2((float2)(acc20, acc21), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y));
5425 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5426 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5427  vstore2((float2)(acc30, acc31), 0, (__global float *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y));
5428 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5429 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
5430 }
5431 
5432 #if defined(ARM_COMPUTE_OPENCL_FP16_ENABLED)
5433 
5482 __kernel void gemm_mm_floating_point_f16_bifrost_acc32(IMAGE_DECLARATION(src0),
5483  IMAGE_DECLARATION(src1),
5484 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
5485  VECTOR_DECLARATION(src2),
5486 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
5487  IMAGE_DECLARATION(dst),
5488  uint src0_stride_z,
5489  uint src1_stride_z,
5490  uint dst_stride_z
5491 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5492  ,
5493  uint src_cross_plane_pad
5494 #endif // REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D
5495 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
5496  ,
5497  uint dst_cross_plane_pad
5498 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
5499  )
5500 {
5501  int idx = get_global_id(0) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X;
5502 
5503  // Compute starting address for matrix A and Matrix B
5504  int2 src_addr = ((int2)(src0_offset_first_element_in_bytes, src1_offset_first_element_in_bytes));
5505 
5506  // Update address for the matrix A
5507  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(1) * src0_stride_y * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y;
5508 
5509  // Update address for the matrix B
5510  src_addr.s1 += idx * sizeof(half);
5511 
5512 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5513  // Since we load a 2D input tile from a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
5514  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
5515  //
5516  // | |
5517  // | plane0 |
5518  // | |
5519  // |__________________|
5520  // |******************|
5521  // | cross_plane_pad |
5522  // |******************|
5523  // | |
5524  // | plane1 |
5525  // | |
5526  // |__________________|
5527 
5528  // The plane (zin) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
5529  uint4 zin = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
5530  zin = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zin);
5531 
5532  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
5533  zin *= (src_cross_plane_pad * src0_stride_y);
5534 
5535  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
5536  // multiply src0_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
5537  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(2) * src0_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
5538 
5539 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5540 
5541  // Add offset for batched GEMM
5542  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(2) * src0_stride_z;
5543 
5544 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5545 
5546 #if defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
5547  // Do not slide matrix B if the matrix B has 3 dimensions and matrix A more than 3
5548  src_addr.s1 += (get_global_id(2) % MATRIX_B_DEPTH) * src1_stride_z;
5549 #else // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
5550  src_addr.s1 += get_global_id(2) * src1_stride_z;
5551 #endif // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
5552 
5553  float8 acc0 = 0.0h;
5554 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5555  float8 acc1 = 0.0h;
5556 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5557 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5558  float8 acc2 = 0.0h;
5559 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5560 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5561  float8 acc3 = 0.0h;
5562 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5563 
5564  int i = 0;
5565  for(; i <= ((int)COLS_A - 4); i += 4)
5566  {
5567 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5568  // Load values from matrix A
5569  half4 a0 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y + zin.s0));
5570 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5571  half4 a1 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y + zin.s1));
5572 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5573 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5574  half4 a2 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y + zin.s2));
5575 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5576 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5577  half4 a3 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y + zin.s3));
5578 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5579 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5580  // Load values from matrix A
5581  half4 a0 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y));
5582 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5583  half4 a1 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y));
5584 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5585 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5586  half4 a2 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y));
5587 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5588 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5589  half4 a3 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y));
5590 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5591 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5592 
5593  // Load values from matrix B
5594  float8 b0 = convert_float8(vload8(0, (__global half *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1)));
5595  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5596 
5597  // Accumulate
5598  acc0 = fma(b0, (float8)a0.s0, acc0);
5599 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5600  acc1 = fma(b0, (float8)a1.s0, acc1);
5601 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5602 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5603  acc2 = fma(b0, (float8)a2.s0, acc2);
5604 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5605 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5606  acc3 = fma(b0, (float8)a3.s0, acc3);
5607 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5608 
5609  b0 = convert_float8(vload8(0, (__global half *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1)));
5610  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5611  acc0 = fma(b0, (float8)a0.s1, acc0);
5612 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5613  acc1 = fma(b0, (float8)a1.s1, acc1);
5614 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5615 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5616  acc2 = fma(b0, (float8)a2.s1, acc2);
5617 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5618 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5619  acc3 = fma(b0, (float8)a3.s1, acc3);
5620 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5621 
5622  b0 = convert_float8(vload8(0, (__global half *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1)));
5623  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5624  acc0 = fma(b0, (float8)a0.s2, acc0);
5625 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5626  acc1 = fma(b0, (float8)a1.s2, acc1);
5627 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5628 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5629  acc2 = fma(b0, (float8)a2.s2, acc2);
5630 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5631 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5632  acc3 = fma(b0, (float8)a3.s2, acc3);
5633 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5634 
5635  b0 = convert_float8(vload8(0, (__global half *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1)));
5636  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5637  acc0 = fma(b0, (float8)a0.s3, acc0);
5638 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5639  acc1 = fma(b0, (float8)a1.s3, acc1);
5640 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5641 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5642  acc2 = fma(b0, (float8)a2.s3, acc2);
5643 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5644 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5645  acc3 = fma(b0, (float8)a3.s3, acc3);
5646 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5647 
5648  src_addr.s0 += 4 * sizeof(half);
5649  }
5650 
5651  for(; i < (int)COLS_A; ++i)
5652  {
5653 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5654  // Load values from matrix A
5655  half a0 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y + zin.s0));
5656 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5657  half a1 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y + zin.s1));
5658 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5659 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5660  half a2 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y + zin.s2));
5661 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5662 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5663  half a3 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y + zin.s3));
5664 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5665 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5666  // Load values from matrix A
5667  half a0 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y));
5668 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5669  half a1 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y));
5670 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5671 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5672  half a2 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y));
5673 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5674 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5675  half a3 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y));
5676 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5677 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5678 
5679  // Load values from matrix B
5680  float8 b0 = convert_float8(vload8(0, (__global half *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1)));
5681 
5682  src_addr += (int2)(sizeof(half), src1_stride_y);
5683 
5684  // Accumulate
5685  acc0 = fma(b0, (float8)a0, acc0); // b0 * (half8)a0;
5686 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5687  acc1 = fma(b0, (float8)a1, acc1); // b0 * (half8)a1;
5688 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5689 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5690  acc2 = fma(b0, (float8)a2, acc2); // b0 * (half8)a2;
5691 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5692 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5693  acc3 = fma(b0, (float8)a3, acc3); // b0 * (half8)a3;
5694 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5695  }
5696 
5697  // Multiply by the weight of matrix-matrix product and store the result
5698 #if defined(ALPHA)
5699  half8 hacc0 = convert_half8(acc0) * (half8)ALPHA;
5700 #else //defined(ALPHA)
5701  half8 hacc0 = convert_half8(acc0);
5702 #endif // defined(ALPHA)
5703 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5704 #if defined(ALPHA)
5705  half8 hacc1 = convert_half8(acc1) * (half8)ALPHA;
5706 #else //defined(ALPHA)
5707  half8 hacc1 = convert_half8(acc1);
5708 #endif //defined(ALPHA)
5709 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y
5710 
5711 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5712 #if defined(ALPHA)
5713  half8 hacc2 = convert_half8(acc2) * (half8)ALPHA;
5714 #else //defined(ALPHA)
5715  half8 hacc2 = convert_half8(acc2);
5716 #endif //defined(ALPHA)
5717 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5718 
5719 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5720 #if defined(ALPHA)
5721  half8 hacc3 = convert_half8(acc3) * (half8)ALPHA;
5722 #else //defined(ALPHA)
5723  half8 hacc3 = convert_half8(acc3);
5724 #endif // defined(ALPHA)
5725 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5726 
5727 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
5728  // *INDENT-OFF*
5729  // clang-format off
5730  __global half *src2_addr = (__global half *)(src2_ptr + src2_offset_first_element_in_bytes + get_global_id(0) * src2_step_x);
5731  half8 c0 = vload8(0, src2_addr);
5732  // clang-format on
5733  // *INDENT-ON*
5734 
5735  hacc0 += c0;
5736 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5737  hacc1 += c0;
5738 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5739 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5740  hacc2 += c0;
5741 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5742 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5743  hacc3 += c0;
5744 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5745 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
5746 
5747  int z = get_global_id(2);
5748 
5749  // Compute destination address
5750  Image dst = CONVERT_TO_IMAGE_STRUCT(dst);
5751 
5752  // Compute dst address
5753  __global uchar *dst_addr = offset(&dst, 0, 0);
5754 
5755 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
5756  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
5757  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
5758  //
5759  // | |
5760  // | plane0 |
5761  // | |
5762  // |__________________|
5763  // |******************|
5764  // | cross_plane_pad |
5765  // |******************|
5766  // | |
5767  // | plane1 |
5768  // | |
5769  // |__________________|
5770 
5771  // The plane (zout) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
5772  uint4 zout = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
5773  zout = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zout);
5774 
5775  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
5776  zout *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
5777 
5778  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
5779  // multiply dst_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
5780  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
5781 
5782  // Store the output block
5783  vstore8(hacc0, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y + zout.s0));
5784 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5785  vstore8(hacc1, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y + zout.s1));
5786 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5787 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5788  vstore8(hacc2, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y + zout.s2));
5789 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5790 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5791  vstore8(hacc3, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y + zout.s3));
5792 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5793 
5794 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
5795  // Add offset for batched GEMM
5796  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z;
5797 
5798  // Store the output block
5799  vstore8(hacc0, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y));
5800 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5801  vstore8(hacc1, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y));
5802 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5803 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5804  vstore8(hacc2, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y));
5805 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5806 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5807  vstore8(hacc3, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y));
5808 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5809 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
5810 }
5811 
5861 __kernel void gemm_mm_floating_point_f16_bifrost(IMAGE_DECLARATION(src0),
5862  IMAGE_DECLARATION(src1),
5863 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
5864  VECTOR_DECLARATION(src2),
5865 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
5866  IMAGE_DECLARATION(dst),
5867  uint src0_stride_z,
5868  uint src1_stride_z,
5869  uint dst_stride_z
5870 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5871  ,
5872  uint src_cross_plane_pad
5873 #endif // REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D
5874 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
5875  ,
5876  uint dst_cross_plane_pad
5877 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
5878  )
5879 {
5880  int idx = get_global_id(0) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X;
5881 
5882  // Compute starting address for matrix A and Matrix B
5883  int2 src_addr = ((int2)(src0_offset_first_element_in_bytes, src1_offset_first_element_in_bytes));
5884 
5885  // Update address for the matrix A
5886  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(1) * src0_stride_y * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y;
5887 
5888  // Update address for the matrix B
5889  src_addr.s1 += idx * sizeof(half);
5890 
5891 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5892  // Since we load a 2D input tile from a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
5893  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
5894  //
5895  // | |
5896  // | plane0 |
5897  // | |
5898  // |__________________|
5899  // |******************|
5900  // | cross_plane_pad |
5901  // |******************|
5902  // | |
5903  // | plane1 |
5904  // | |
5905  // |__________________|
5906 
5907  // The plane (zin) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
5908  uint4 zin = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
5909  zin = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zin);
5910 
5911  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
5912  zin *= (src_cross_plane_pad * src0_stride_y);
5913 
5914  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
5915  // multiply src0_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
5916  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(2) * src0_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
5917 
5918 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5919 
5920  // Add offset for batched GEMM
5921  src_addr.s0 += get_global_id(2) * src0_stride_z;
5922 
5923 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5924 
5925 #if defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
5926  // Do not slide matrix B if the matrix B has 3 dimensions and matrix A more than 3
5927  src_addr.s1 += (get_global_id(2) % MATRIX_B_DEPTH) * src1_stride_z;
5928 #else // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
5929  src_addr.s1 += get_global_id(2) * src1_stride_z;
5930 #endif // defined(MATRIX_B_DEPTH)
5931 
5932  half8 acc0 = 0.0h;
5933 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5934  half8 acc1 = 0.0h;
5935 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5936 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5937  half8 acc2 = 0.0h;
5938 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5939 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5940  half8 acc3 = 0.0h;
5941 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5942 
5943  int i = 0;
5944  for(; i <= ((int)COLS_A - 4); i += 4)
5945  {
5946 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5947  // Load values from matrix A
5948  half4 a0 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y + zin.s0));
5949 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5950  half4 a1 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y + zin.s1));
5951 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5952 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5953  half4 a2 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y + zin.s2));
5954 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5955 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5956  half4 a3 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y + zin.s3));
5957 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5958 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5959  // Load values from matrix A
5960  half4 a0 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y));
5961 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5962  half4 a1 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y));
5963 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5964 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5965  half4 a2 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y));
5966 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5967 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5968  half4 a3 = vload4(0, (__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y));
5969 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5970 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
5971 
5972  // Load values from matrix B
5973  half8 b0 = vload8(0, (__global half *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
5974  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5975 
5976  // Accumulate
5977  acc0 = fma(b0, (half8)a0.s0, acc0);
5978 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5979  acc1 = fma(b0, (half8)a1.s0, acc1);
5980 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5981 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5982  acc2 = fma(b0, (half8)a2.s0, acc2);
5983 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5984 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5985  acc3 = fma(b0, (half8)a3.s0, acc3);
5986 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5987 
5988  b0 = vload8(0, (__global half *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
5989  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
5990  acc0 = fma(b0, (half8)a0.s1, acc0);
5991 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5992  acc1 = fma(b0, (half8)a1.s1, acc1);
5993 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
5994 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5995  acc2 = fma(b0, (half8)a2.s1, acc2);
5996 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
5997 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
5998  acc3 = fma(b0, (half8)a3.s1, acc3);
5999 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6000 
6001  b0 = vload8(0, (__global half *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
6002  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
6003  acc0 = fma(b0, (half8)a0.s2, acc0);
6004 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6005  acc1 = fma(b0, (half8)a1.s2, acc1);
6006 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6007 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6008  acc2 = fma(b0, (half8)a2.s2, acc2);
6009 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6010 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6011  acc3 = fma(b0, (half8)a3.s2, acc3);
6012 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6013 
6014  b0 = vload8(0, (__global half *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
6015  src_addr.s1 += src1_stride_y;
6016  acc0 = fma(b0, (half8)a0.s3, acc0);
6017 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6018  acc1 = fma(b0, (half8)a1.s3, acc1);
6019 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6020 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6021  acc2 = fma(b0, (half8)a2.s3, acc2);
6022 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6023 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6024  acc3 = fma(b0, (half8)a3.s3, acc3);
6025 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6026 
6027  src_addr.s0 += 4 * sizeof(half);
6028  }
6029 
6030  for(; i < (int)COLS_A; ++i)
6031  {
6032 #if defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
6033  // Load values from matrix A
6034  half a0 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y + zin.s0));
6035 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6036  half a1 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y + zin.s1));
6037 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6038 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6039  half a2 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y + zin.s2));
6040 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6041 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6042  half a3 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y + zin.s3));
6043 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6044 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
6045  // Load values from matrix A
6046  half a0 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 0 * src0_stride_y));
6047 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6048  half a1 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 1 * src0_stride_y));
6049 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6050 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6051  half a2 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 2 * src0_stride_y));
6052 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6053 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6054  half a3 = *((__global half *)(src0_ptr + src_addr.s0 + 3 * src0_stride_y));
6055 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6056 #endif // defined(REINTERPRET_INPUT_AS_3D)
6057 
6058  // Load values from matrix B
6059  half8 b0 = vload8(0, (__global half *)(src1_ptr + src_addr.s1));
6060 
6061  src_addr += (int2)(sizeof(half), src1_stride_y);
6062 
6063  // Accumulate
6064  acc0 = fma(b0, (half8)a0, acc0); // b0 * (half8)a0;
6065 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6066  acc1 = fma(b0, (half8)a1, acc1); // b0 * (half8)a1;
6067 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6068 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6069  acc2 = fma(b0, (half8)a2, acc2); // b0 * (half8)a2;
6070 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6071 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6072  acc3 = fma(b0, (half8)a3, acc3); // b0 * (half8)a3;
6073 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6074  }
6075 
6076  // Multiply by the weight of matrix-matrix product and store the result
6077 #if defined(ALPHA)
