6078  acc0 = acc0 * (half8)ALPHA;
6079 #endif // defined(ALPHA)
6080 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1 && defined(ALPHA)
6081  acc1 = acc1 * (half8)ALPHA;
6082 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1 && defined(ALPHA)
6083 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2 && defined(ALPHA)
6084  acc2 = acc2 * (half8)ALPHA;
6085 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2 && defined(ALPHA)
6086 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3 && defined(ALPHA)
6087  acc3 = acc3 * (half8)ALPHA;
6088 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3 && defined(ALPHA)
6089 
6090 #if defined(ADD_VEC_C)
6091  // *INDENT-OFF*
6092  // clang-format off
6093  __global half *src2_addr = (__global half *)(src2_ptr + src2_offset_first_element_in_bytes + get_global_id(0) * src2_step_x);
6094  half8 c0 = vload8(0, src2_addr);
6095  // clang-format on
6096  // *INDENT-ON*
6097 
6098  acc0 += c0;
6099 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6100  acc1 += c0;
6101 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6102 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6103  acc2 += c0;
6104 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6105 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6106  acc3 += c0;
6107 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6108 #endif /* defined(ADD_VEC_C) */
6109 
6110  int z = get_global_id(2);
6111 
6112  // Compute destination address
6113  Image dst = CONVERT_TO_IMAGE_STRUCT(dst);
6114 
6115  // Compute dst address
6116  __global uchar *dst_addr = offset(&dst, 0, 0);
6117 
6118 #if defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
6119  // Since we store a 2D output tile in a 3D tensor, we need to check when the plane changes across the z dimension
6120  // in order to take into account the presence of possible cross plane paddings
6121  //
6122  // | |
6123  // | plane0 |
6124  // | |
6125  // |__________________|
6126  // |******************|
6127  // | cross_plane_pad |
6128  // |******************|
6129  // | |
6130  // | plane1 |
6131  // | |
6132  // |__________________|
6133 
6134  // The plane (zout) is calculated dividing M (get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y) by HEIGHT_GEMM3D
6135  uint4 zout = ((uint4)(0, 1, 2, 3) + (uint4)(get_global_id(1) * NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y)) / (uint4)HEIGHT_GEMM3D;
6136  zout = min(DEPTH_GEMM3D - 1, zout);
6137 
6138  // Add offset due to the cross plane paddings
6139  zout *= (dst_cross_plane_pad * dst_stride_y);
6140 
6141  // Add offset for batched GEMM. The batches will be in the fourth dimension and for this reason we
6142  // multiply dst_stride_z by DEPTH_GEMM3D
6143  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z * DEPTH_GEMM3D;
6144 
6145  // Store the output block
6146  vstore8(acc0, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y + zout.s0));
6147 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6148  vstore8(acc1, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y + zout.s1));
6149 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6150 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6151  vstore8(acc2, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y + zout.s2));
6152 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6153 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6154  vstore8(acc3, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y + zout.s3));
6155 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6156 
6157 #else // defined(REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D)
6158  // Add offset for batched GEMM
6159  dst_addr += z * dst_stride_z;
6160 
6161  // Store the output block
6162  vstore8(acc0, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 0 * dst_stride_y));
6163 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6164  vstore8(acc1, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 1 * dst_stride_y));
6165 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 1
6166 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6167  vstore8(acc2, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 2 * dst_stride_y));
6168 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 2
6169 #if NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6170  vstore8(acc3, 0, (__global half *)(dst_addr + 3 * dst_stride_y));
6171 #endif // NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y > 3
6172 #endif // REINTERPRET_OUTPUT_AS_3D
6173 }
6174 #endif // defined(ARM_COMPUTE_OPENCL_FP16_ENABLED)
6175 
6176 #endif // defined(COLS_A) && defined(NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_X) && (NUM_ELEMS_PROCESSED_PER_THREAD_Y)

6179 
6200 __kernel void gemm_ma_f32(TENSOR3D_DECLARATION(src),
6201  TENSOR3D_DECLARATION(dst))
6202 {
6203  // Compute source and destination addresses
6204  Tensor3D src = CONVERT_TO_TENSOR3D_STRUCT(src);
6205  Tensor3D dst = CONVERT_TO_TENSOR3D_STRUCT(dst);
6206 
6207  // Load values from A x B
6208  float4 alpha_ab = vload4(0, (__global float *)dst.ptr);
6209 
6210  // Load values from Matrix C
